Important News Two

Communists in Hukou Have Been Repelled 73

Jiujiang Communication: The communist bandits Fang Zhimin, Shao Shiping, etc., after being severely beaten by government troops in Raozhou, led 5,000 to 6,000 bandits on the 4th of this month and fled to the Jiangqiao area of Hukou, hoping to disrupt Xunhu. Zhang Chao, the battalion commander of the Special Service Battalion of the 18th Jiangxi Division and the commander of the 2nd Garrison Regiment, led more than 2,000 soldiers from Duchang to pursue and suppress them. Commander Tong of the 1st Battalion of the 2nd Regiment of the Ministry of Finance's Anti-Smuggling Unit also led his troops to intercept them at 4:00 AM that day. When they arrived at Lantingling, they made contact with the bandits and immediately repelled them. They continued to pursue them to Jiangqiao, where they engaged in fierce fighting. They used machine guns and automatic rifles to fire fiercely, causing about 400 to 500 casualties on the bandit side. Wang Xinqu, the commander of the Command Headquarters of the Ministry of Finance's Anti-Smuggling Unit, arrived at 4:00 PM to inspect the defense area. Hearing that Commander Tong was in contact with the bandits, he went to the front to command. Commander Wang believed that the bandits were powerful and our army was outnumbered. Therefore, he telegraphed Chairman Lu, requesting him to quickly send a large army to pursue and suppress them. At the same time, he reorganized his troops, firmly defended the county seat, and deployed troops to guard all important places. After completing the deployment, he returned to Xunzhen at 5:00 PM on the 5th. In this battle, the bandits had 5,000 to 6,000 troops, and Wang's troops were less than two battalions. He managed to repel the bandits, allowing Hukou to be preserved. His fighting spirit is truly admirable. (September 8th)

Russian Red Party Plans to Bomb the Songhua River Railway Bridge 74

Binjiang Police Arrest Fourteen Members of the Russian Red Party Harbin Communication: On the afternoon of August 31st, Gao Qidong, the director of the Binjiang Public Security Bureau, received a confidential report stating that a group of Russian Communists were planning to disrupt the area along the river and planned to blow up the Songhua River Railway Bridge to create red terror. They hired a No. 37 sailing boat and falsely claimed to be going to Heihe. The bureau had heard of this news a week ago and had been paying attention to preventing it. After receiving the report, he immediately ordered his officers to arrest Li, the owner of the No. 37 sailing boat, from the eastern suburbs of Harbin. The director interrogated him, and he confessed that the Russians had hired the boat. There were about ten of them, all young men in their twenties. They claimed to be going to the lower reaches of the river to transport machinery and agricultural implements, but before sailing, they had to go to the Hengjiang Great Railway Bridge north of the river to pick up items. They stated that the boat fare was 100 yuan, and they paid 25 yuan in advance. Li insisted on paying half the amount in advance, so they had not yet reached an agreement. After Gao obtained the confession, he ordered the captain of the detective team, Gao Changsan, to investigate strictly. Gao sent detectives Zhang Minglun and Ma Jiuzhai to pose as boatmen and serve on the No. 37 sailing boat. At 6:00 PM on September 1st, a group of about seventeen Russians, each carrying luggage, arrived at the dock at Qidaojiekou and hailed a ferry. Detectives Zhang and Ma solicited business and tricked the group of Russians onto the No. 37 sailing boat. They immediately hoisted the sails and sailed out of the city. In the middle of the river, they pretended to have a broken rudder and stopped to repair it. At that time, the detective team and the security team had received reports separately and knew that the Russians had been caught. The captain of the security team, Jin, and the captain of the detective team, Gao, led dozens of detectives and police officers in a motorboat to pursue them. Guan Zhongxing, the director of the Water Police Bureau, also took a gunboat and led a large team of police officers to set out. At 6:30 PM, they approached the sailing boat and fired a warning shot, ordering the Russians to raise their hands. The Russians ignored them. Some of them took out grenades from their bags and tried to throw them at the police boat. Detectives Ma and Zhang drew their guns to stop them. The police team boarded the boat and tied up the Russians one by one. They searched them and found a long, cylindrical, highly explosive grenade on each of them. They were immediately escorted to the Binjiang Public Security Bureau. After being interrogated by Director Gao Qidong, their statements were inconsistent. Two of them claimed to be White Russians and were ordered by Zhang Zongchang to go to the Heihe area to do business. When asked what kind of business, they refused to answer. The case will be tried in court within days, but according to official proof, they are purely international communists who are plotting to disrupt North Manchuria. (1st)

Quick News from Wuhu 75

Yesterday, wounded soldiers from the Datong Injured Soldiers Hospital clashed with the security team sent by the Provincial Security Office. The wounded soldiers seized the firearms of the anti-smuggling police, and the two sides exchanged fire. The company commander of the security team was shot and fell into the water and died. Soldiers on both sides were also injured, and several civilians were injured by stray bullets. Later, a warship opened fire to suppress the situation, and it returned to peace. In addition to sending more security teams to the area, the provincial government also sent two companies of the Wuhu Garrison Regiment to suppress the situation today.

Political News Chen Tiaoyuan has been reinstated as the chairman of Anhui Province and has arrived in Beijing from the front. However, Chen feels deeply that the finances of Anhui Province are exhausted, and it is difficult to manage the finances unless the position of Special Commissioner for Finance is concurrently held by the Director of the Finance Department. He is currently in discussions with the National Government and is expected to take office in Anhui in about two weeks.

Today is the anniversary of the Treaty of Xin Chou. For the sake of local security, the authorities advised against gatherings and parades in advance, so there were no activities in various circles. Since last night, the military and police have been inspecting pedestrians on the roads, streets, and North Gate, and the security is very strict today.

The bandits in Wuhua Mountain, Fanchang County, were again killed by the 3rd Battalion of the Garrison Regiment, and more than 20 rifles were seized. The bandits have been gradually suppressed. Yesterday, the battalion also cooperated with various circles in Fanchang to cut down all the trees on Wuhua Mountain to prevent bandits from hiding. (September 7th)

This morning, the Wuhu Liji Company's Wuhu-Datong small wheel, carrying passengers from Wuhu to Datong, was intercepted by more than 20 bandits with weapons while passing through the Longxingzhou area of Digang. They opened fire and forced the ship to stop, then rushed aboard and searched the passengers one by one, looting more than 8,000 yuan in cash, mostly carried by rice merchants. Fortunately, the passengers were not injured. The Wuhu Shipping Association has reported the incident to the military and police authorities and requested their arrest.

The provincial government has decided to establish a Provincial Gazetteer Preparatory Office and has appointed Jiang Tonghou as the director of the Preparatory Office. It is scheduled to be established on September 16th. The funds will be provided by adding 1% to the land tax, deed tax, tooth tax, livestock tax, and slaughter tax in various counties. Orders have been telegraphed to the county governments to comply.

The 3rd Battalion of the Garrison Regiment, which was sent to Fanchang to suppress the bandits, has almost completely annihilated the bandits in Wuhua Mountain. Yesterday, they also arrested seven suspects, including Lu Boxun, Yu Zhengshan, and Zhou Guoquan, at Pinggoupu and escorted them to Wuhu today for interrogation by the regiment headquarters. (September 8th)

Local Communication

Songjiang 76

Investigation into the Tragic Death of Tang Zhi Kui The owner of Tang Helong store, Tang Zhikui, was stabbed to death by a thief at two o'clock in the morning on the fifth, with fifteen large and small knife wounds. After the prosecutor arrived to inspect and filled out the corpse form, an order was issued to arrest the murderer. However, on the night of Tang Zhikui's tragic death, he stayed in the store. After the incident, a careful examination of the murderer's entry and exit routes showed only footprints going out, but no signs of entry. The front shop was obviously not accessible to outsiders, and the garden doors in the back were all locked. From the bedroom to the back door, there were more than a dozen doors, either bolted or locked, all of which were opened one by one, allowing the murderer to escape calmly in the darkness. Therefore, these various doubts have aroused speculation in society. The family has submitted a petition to the County Court Prosecutor's Office, offering a reward for the arrest of the murderer. Today (the 9th), the Prosecutor's Office issued summons to Tang Cai, the widow of the deceased, his son Qiu Sheng, his nephew Jingren (who served as the store's accountant), and Ye Diku, a student who shared a room with him, to investigate everything in order to arrest the murderer. Military Department Sends Committee to Investigate Military Property The Military Administration Department has sent Zhang Mingda and several other investigators from the Construction Division of the Military Supply Department to Songjiang to organize an office at Xiaobei Temple as members of the Second District Investigation Area for the Clearance of Military Property in Jiangsu Province, and will be responsible for investigating military property in this county. The office has now begun operations and has recently consulted the county government, stating that according to Article 14, Paragraph 1 of the Regulations on the Management of Military Property, anyone who encroaches upon, steals, sells, conceals, or illegally obtains military property, or forges licenses, will be severely punished in addition to the recovery of the military property. However, those who confess before being discovered will be exempt from punishment, except for the recovery of the military property. County Magistrate Jin has issued orders to his subordinates to inform them accordingly.

Oil Mill Owner Receives Threatening Letters Repeatedly The owner of the Shen oil mill in Yanjiawan in the county received threatening letters in the spring, demanding 500 yuan. The other day, he received another letter from bandits demanding 1,300 yuan, with a date to meet in Shanghai. At the time, the owner's younger brother went to Shanghai for business and stayed at the Jiuhua Hotel. As soon as he unpacked his luggage, another letter from the bandits arrived, with even more激烈的措词。 The Garrison Department Sends Troops to Take Over Defense This city has always been guarded by a special regiment from the Anti-Smuggling Bureau. Now, due to successive transfers, the Shanghai Garrison Headquarters has transferred the 1st Battalion of the 2nd Supplementary Regiment of the 5th Division to Songjiang to take over the defense. They arrived in Songjiang today.

Trial Scheduled for Reactionary Case: Two reporters from a certain newspaper in Changshu, Gui Han and Shen Xuexia, were accused by the county party headquarters of having counter-revolutionary suspicions. The Lixing Steamboat on the Shenhu Route Robbed: The Lixing steamboat, which travels between Shanghai and Huzhou, set off from Shanghai at about 2:00 AM the day before yesterday (the 8th). When it was passing the Yuhui Xiehutang area near Jiashan, it was suddenly ambushed by a large gang of pirate ships, about twenty or more, with about two hundred or more pirates. Fengxian 78

The Police Team's Investigation of the Reactionary Case: The county police team has investigated the reactionary activities of various squad leaders and police officers. We have already reported on this in our newspaper. Now we have learned that this matter started when Meng Jiluo, who once served as the squad leader of the first squad, was entrusted by a certain northern warlord to come to Fengxian to campaign and to issue appointment certificates indiscriminately to recruit people widely, with Zhou Bingrong, the deputy squad leader of the general headquarters, as the leader to take charge of the liaison. As a result, many squads were incited by him. However, the actions of these people were inevitably strange on weekdays, so acting team leader Tu had already paid attention to them. Last Wednesday, the general headquarters accidentally found a letter from Pan Jisheng, who claimed to be a brigade commander, sent from Shanghai to Zhou Bingrong. The content stated that "Our army has been established and now has 8,000 rifles and hundreds of box cannons. We will set off soon, but the army commander is in Tianjin on official business, so I hope that all brothers will not be impatient," At the same time, Yang Xingsheng, the second squad leader stationed in Zhuang, also secretly reported to the team that Pan Adong had secretly come to plot rebellion. Acting team leader Tu was handling the matter together when suddenly Chen Shu, the squad leader of the general headquarters, reported that the reactionary liaison Meng Jiluo had arrived in the south. So he immediately acted without a sound and arrested him at a certain tavern on South Street and sent him directly to the County Public Security Bureau. He and Director Li Zhibin secretly interrogated him, and he directly admitted that he had come to Fengxian to campaign and had appointed someone as the fake commander of the regiment, battalion, and company, and on the spot, they found in his possession an order from the fake brigade commander Pan Jisheng, ordering the fake commander Zhou Bingrong to start an uprising from that day on. After the interrogation, Tu and Li were afraid that the news would leak out, so they immediately sent trusted soldiers overnight to the residence of the fourth squad to arrest all the confessed criminals. A total of seven people, including squad leaders Mao Rongfa and Zhao Desheng, were arrested one after another and were transferred to the Shanghai Songhu Garrison Command for handling today (the 8th) by the county with official documents.

The County Government Executes Bandits by Firing Squad: The county government received a telegram from the provincial government stating that Chen Siming and five other bandits who robbed Yu Huolin's house in Zhuanghekou in the county had confessed to the crime and should be sentenced to death. County Magistrate Shen dispatched Secretary Yang Shudu this morning (the 8th) to supervise the police team in verifying the identities of the criminals and moved them to the open space of the Baijia Ancestral Hall for execution according to law. Chen Siming, 28 years old, Song Fengxiang, 20 years old, Wu Baotian, 40 years old, Fang Guoliang, 24 years old, and Lu Xiaodi, 29 years old, were executed by firing squad.

Jiangyin 79

County Party Headquarters Orders the Sealing of Newspaper Offices: The County Party Headquarters Rectification Committee recently submitted a request to the Provincial Party Committee, stating that the Jiangyin Minsheng and Shangbao newspapers had both violated Articles 8 and 9 of the Guiding Principles for News Reporting. The 61st meeting of the Provincial Rectification Committee had decided to close them down. (Note: Minsheng had already ceased publication on the 3rd due to economic reasons, but Shangbao had not stopped publishing.) On the morning of the 9th, Qi Jiewen, the main editor of Shangbao, Zhu Shuping, a staff member (assistant of the First District Office), Jiewen's younger brother Songwen, the head of the First District, and Meng Linyun, a servant, were all arrested.

Detention of Former Director Dai to Calculate Representative Accounts: Dai Yuandu, the former director of the Finance Bureau, sent his brother Dai Jing to Cheng to calculate the accounts of the handover. At 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 8th, he convened a meeting of representatives from various bureaus to calculate local expenses. At that time, it was found that the Finance Bureau had collected 7,500 yuan in interest from various banks and shops last year, which was handed over to the County Local Assets Department. It was not stated which agency issued the loan note, nor was it stated what the money was used for. Later, at the end of the year, the Finance Bureau allocated more than 400 yuan from the education item and more than 3,000 yuan of additional taxes from the construction item, together with the local additional taxes, and returned them to the banks and shops. This was not in compliance with the procedures, so the calculation did not yield results. The representatives of the Education and Construction Bureaus immediately appealed to County Magistrate Li, who ordered the Public Security Bureau to detain Dai Jing temporarily.

Two Grandsons of the Xie Family Kidnapped: Xie Fulin and Xie Rulin, rent collectors of Miao Fuyan in Shengang Township, who lived in Shunbei Township, were kidnapped by several bandits the night before last. Rulin, 16, and his grandson, 11, were taken away, and a ransom of 3,000 yuan was demanded for their return.

Wuxi 80

筹设皋桥大电厂

Planning the Establishment of the Gaoqiao Power Plant: The National Government Construction Commission, in order to develop the electricity industry, convened responsible personnel from various directly-administered power plants in Beijing a month ago for a meeting. It was decided to build a large power plant in both Jiangbei and Jiangnan. The large power plant in Jiangbei was decided to be located on the shore of Hongze Lake, and the large power plant in Jiangnan was decided to be centered in Wuxi, gradually expanding to neighboring counties. Recently, the commission specially sent technician Wu to Wuxi to survey the area. As a result of the survey, it was found that the area near Gaoqiao was the most suitable for building a plant. Technician Wu reported the results of the survey to the Construction Commission, and then Bao Guobao, the director of the electrical department of the commission, came to Wuxi for a re-survey, which was also considered satisfactory. Currently, specific plans for the construction of the plant are being properly drafted, and it is planned to purchase land and invite bids for the construction of the plant within the year. When the Gaoqiao power plant is established in the future, the electricity price will be low, so that all factories can use electricity as power, so that the entire county of Wuxi can be industrialized and electrified. It is also heard that in order to facilitate the transportation of coal for the power plant, Director Bao has reported to the Construction Commission and consulted the Ministry of Railways, ordering the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway Bureau to set up the planned small station between Wuxi and Shitangwan in Gaoqiao to facilitate transportation. Otherwise, a branch road will be added to Meijing (about three or four li from Gaoqiao) to directly reach Gaoqiao from Meijing.

The Rampancy of Bandits Is Worrying: In recent months, robbery cases have occurred frequently in the townships of this county, and few have been solved, so the atmosphere of banditry is becoming increasingly rampant. The day before yesterday at midnight, the home of Meng Bangjie, a resident of Yantai Township in the Sixth District, was suddenly broken into by more than a dozen bandits with guns. They entered the house and carried out a robbery, tying up all the members of the Meng family and searching for two hours before firing two shots into the air as a warning and leaving. In this incident, clothing and other items worth about 600 yuan were robbed. The Deadline for Resolving the Fraud and Breach of Trust Case: Liu Hanzhang, the owner of Fulongxing Leather Shoe Store at the entrance of the Shuyuan Alley in the city of this county, and his son Xikang, purchased firearms on behalf of Bian Shang and others, the heads of the Weihu Tuan in Qingyang, Qixia, and Yunting townships of Jiangyin, in June of the 17th year of the Republic of China, totaling 4,200 yuan, but the firearms were never delivered. Bian immediately negotiated with the Liu family, and Liu, knowing that he was at fault, used more than 70 mu of fake land in Suzhou as collateral, with Liu providing a full guarantee. In the spring of the 18th year, because Liu ignored it, Bian filed a complaint with the Wuxi County Government about the facts of fraud, breach of trust, and forgery of official seals. More than a year has passed without any results, which shows the difficulty of litigation. Yesterday, the trial was held by the judge Yu, who ordered the Liu family to settle the matter outside of court, setting a deadline of half a month. If the matter could not be settled, a judgment would be made according to law. The Liu family obeyed the order and withdrew. It is also heard that the people of the three townships of Yangqing are also concerned that the bandit forces in their townships have recently revived and urgently need firearms to be used. If the case is further delayed, they will jointly file a complaint with the central government and the provincial government.

Reactionary Elements Arrested in Xicang Town: Wang Wenzao, the leader of the second squad of the second company of the police force stationed in the twelfth district (Taibo City, Xicang Town), received a secret report from a citizen the day before yesterday, stating that reactionary elements were hiding in a certain small teahouse in the town, holding secret meetings in the fields every night and posting reactionary slogans, plotting wrongdoing. After receiving the report, Squad Leader Wang immediately led his team to search the address and arrested two reactionary elements, Wang Rengen and Chu Guijin, on the spot, and seized a bundle of reactionary slogans. He immediately led the team to interrogate them and escorted them to the city yesterday to be taken to the brigade headquarters, where Brigade Commander Wang held a preliminary trial. The confessions of the two criminals were extremely cunning, so they immediately prepared a document to transfer them to the county government to await interrogation.

Yangzhou 81

Counter-suit in the Yanghuo Road Incident: On the Yanghuo Road in this county, a disturbance occurred previously due to road workers, who assaulted officials and destroyed the houses of various section chiefs. The house of Dong Shushen, the section chief of the sixteenth section, was also among those destroyed. However, Dong believed that Zhai Yueting and eight others were the instigators and filed separate complaints with the Construction Department and the county government. The county government repeatedly ordered the police team and the second and fourth public security bureaus in charge to strictly arrest them. It is heard that six people, including Xie Zhengfu, have been arrested one after another and handed over to the court for punishment. Dong also believed that the criminals had not been fully arrested and accused Officer Dai of the fourth public security bureau of accepting bribes. The general bureau assigned Inspector Liao Qiang to investigate thoroughly, but there was no evidence of bribery. Dong then accused Liao of also taking bribes. The general bureau has now assigned Inspector Gong to investigate again. At that time, they received an instruction from the Construction Department, stating that Tang Wansan and others, representatives of the thirty-six villages in Hangjiaji, presented that Dong Shushen was a rogue who falsely accused Zhai and the other nine people. Moreover, Dong had collected hundreds of yuan in construction funds on behalf of the workers but had not handed them over to the public, and Dong had issued private receipts as evidence. The Yanghuo Road incident was within the scope of the fifteenth section and had nothing to do with the sixteenth section. They requested that Dong be severely punished for violating the law himself and falsely accusing good citizens. It is hoped that the matter will be investigated and reported back.

Changshu 82

Attempted Robbery near Dayi Bridge: Near Wanfeng Bridge between Dayi Bridge and the port in the western countryside of this county, Zhao Jia area. The villagers in that area mostly engage in fishing. Gu Chen, a 35-year-old woman from Dayi Bridge, whose husband had died of illness, had a son and a daughter, who also relied on aquatic products for a living. Recently, as autumn was approaching, she was building a new boat and had prepared 30 foreign dollars to go to the city to buy bamboo for weaving. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the day before yesterday, three big men quietly boarded Chen's boat, intending to rob her of her money. Chen, seeing this, knew that things were not good and shouted for help. The bandits robbed the foreign dollars and fled ashore. The villagers, hearing the alarm, rushed to chase after them. At the Xiaotang in front, the bandits tried to wade across the water but were caught by the villagers. When the bandits fled, they pushed Chen into the river because they saw her shouting wildly, but fortunately, she was rescued by someone. The three bandits were sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. All three denied that they were thieves, so the plaintiff and defendants were transferred to the city for further investigation.

A Kidnapped Person Returns in the Luhe Town Kidnapping Case: Regarding the incident in Luhe Town on the border of Changtai, where bandits robbed and kidnapped Cui Zhongsan, the owner of a rice shop, and his partners the day before yesterday, it is now known that Cui's partner has been released from the bandit den in Da'an Port and entrusted him to deliver a letter to Cui, to discuss the ransom issue. However, Cui's family has not yet expressed their opinion, and recently the wealthy households in the town have been moving to Changshu one after another.

Nantong 83

Huangqiao Bandit Leader Surrenders: Li Jigen, a notorious bandit who occupies Huangqiao in Jiangbei, has more than 1,600 followers. Commander Li has approved it.

Four Townships Plan to Clear the Countryside: Tong, Ru, Jing, and Tai counties are carrying out a large-scale campaign to suppress bandits. The provincial government is concerned that the bandits will be difficult to eliminate, so it has ordered the four counties to imitate the Qingxiang measures in the Taihu Lake area and carry out the campaign on a regular basis. It is heard that the county magistrates of the four counties will convene a meeting in Tong within the next few days to discuss preparations.

Warden of the Fourth Prison Replaced: The warden of the Fourth Prison is currently being replaced by Zeng Guochen. The High Court has appointed Sun Xiong to take over. Sun arrived in Tong on the 8th to take office.

Bandit Leader Who Raided Qiantan Town Executed by Firing Squad: In the spring of this year, Qiantan Town was raided by Feng Buzhou, the leader of the Red Fourteenth Army of the False Army. The provincial, county, military, and police searched for the criminal without success. On the 7th, Bandit Feng sneaked back to Erqian and was captured and executed by firing squad by the bandit suppression army.

Rugao 84

Wang Yuwen Executed in Huangqiao: Wang Yuwen, the leader of the Communist Party in this county, was from Zhujiazhuang in Lugang District of this county. He was the stepson of Zhu Guixin and was about 25 or 26 years old. He graduated from the second generation of Rugao and the Shanghai Longmen Second Normal School. When the National Revolutionary Army arrived in Rugao in the 16th year, he served as a staff member of the Youth Department of the County Party Headquarters and later as a member of the Public Security Section of the Lugang District Administrative Bureau. Wang also joined the May 1st Jianglu Riot and arbitrarily burned and killed people in the western countryside. The county government of this county had offered a reward of 1,000 yuan for his arrest. After Xu Fangde, Wu Yasu, and others were executed, Wang Yingchao, Tang Shiren, and others also fled far away upon hearing the news. Wang used the alias Lao Ding to direct the riots in the western countryside and traveled between Shanghai and Rugao to provide military supplies, serving as a special commissioner of the false five counties. The day before yesterday, Yang Tingfang, the captain of the second battalion of the provincial police team stationed in Huangqiao, reported based on the report of the surrendered bandit leader Li Jigen and served as a mole, arresting Wang in a certain village west of Luzhuang. He was immediately taken to Huangqiao and beheaded, and his head was immediately taken to Luzhuang to be displayed to the public.

Pinghu 85

Xinhuang Ferry Boat Robbed at Xiangong Temple: Xiangong Temple is located outside the West Gate of Pingyi, about four or five li from the city, close to Jingtu Temple, and belongs to the territory of Jiayi. This is the only route from Pinghu to Xinhuang Town. The ferry boat owner is named Cao Erguan. He travels back and forth every day and is reliable. Therefore, many shops entrust him to carry silver dollars. Yesterday (the 7th) morning, the boat sailed from Xinkai Ping and passed in front of Xiangong Temple. Two bandits were standing on the shore. One bandit called out to catch the boat. The boat owner did not think it was strange and immediately brought the boat ashore. Unexpectedly, after the bandit boarded the boat, he fired a shot into the air at the bow of the boat. The bandit on the shore also pointed a pistol at the rower and ordered him to stop rowing. As a result, the banknotes and silver dollars in Cao Erguan's money bag, totaling more than 600 yuan, were all robbed. The two thieves waited on the shore until the boat had rowed far away before they ran away, apparently wanting the people on the boat not to know their route. Cao Erguan immediately reported to the Pinghu Public Security Bureau. The bureau told him that the incident occurred in Jiaxing County and that he had to report to the Xinhuang Public Security Bureau. Cao Erguan then returned in a state of disarray.

Tai Bao A Shu's Fierce Lieutenant Captured: Xi Zhangsheng, a notorious bandit on the border of Jin and Ping, nicknamed "Gunpowder Bag," was a lieutenant under Tai Bao A Shu, falsely claiming to be a battalion commander. He was a fierce bandit. He was captured by Xie Baosheng, the captain of the Jiangsu Water Police Team, the day before yesterday outside the West Gate of Chuansha. During the interrogation, he confessed to organizing the looting of Langxia Town. He has been sent to the Minhang District Department for interrogation.

Huzhou 86

Detective Team Leader Requests Handgun: Hu Rongbin, the leader of the detective team of the Wuxing County Public Security Bureau, is in charge of detective work. If he encounters the arrest of bandits and thieves, he must carry a handgun for self-defense. The handgun he previously received was not enough. Sometimes, although he can temporarily request or borrow one, he is deeply afraid that he will not be able to respond in time in case of an emergency. Therefore, he plans to ask the Director of the Public Security Bureau to give him four more handguns and some bullets for standby use. Director Chen has approved the issuance.

Bandits Send Letters and Demand Money in the Northwest Township: A certain foreman of the Huashang Stone Company lives in Xiaochendu, a place in the northwest township of the Huzhou area. Although he works for the company, his salary is not enough for household expenses. Unexpectedly, a dozen bandits suddenly came to the area at about 12:00 midnight the day before yesterday and fired more than a dozen shots as a warning, and sent letters to the slightly wealthy families. The worker also received a letter from the bandits, reportedly demanding a thousand foreign dollars.

Jiashan 87

Follow-up Interrogation of Two Town Robbery Cases: Tianningzhuang in this county and the Youchegang in Jiaxing were raided by a group of bandits on the 7th. It has been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that Tianningzhuang has been repeatedly robbed and the local area has suffered greatly. Therefore, all businesses in the area went on strike yesterday. Although they were persuaded to return to work, it was still ineffective. The seven kidnapped men and women have not yet been heard from. The two towns conducted a joint inspection for a week. It was later learned that it was the gang of bandits who robbed the Shanghai-Huzhou liner, causing considerable losses, and kidnapped a passenger. A passenger, Zhu, was shot and injured. It is now heard that one of the hostages has been released, Mr. Zhu. The bandit leader sent a message to the other hostages, urging them to redeem themselves quickly.

Bandits Rob Rice Boat in Huajing: Huajing, near Yuhui in this county, is a remote area. Yesterday, suddenly three or forty pirate ships came. Important News: Japanese Students Delay Paying Tuition 88

Tokyo Telegraph, 9th: The intensification of the recession is gradually affecting students' pockets. The number of male and female middle school students in Tokyo and other places who are late in paying tuition has recently increased sharply, especially in private schools. At the beginning of the second semester, various schools have announced the recruitment of a large number of vacancies. The Tokyo Prefectural School Affairs Section is very embarrassed about this and is starting to investigate the actual situation. It is now known that more than 10,000 students have dropped out of school in Tokyo Prefecture alone due to unpaid tuition.

Ministry of Education Orders Again

Free Tuition for Students from Shaanxi, Gansu, Suiyuan, and Chahar 89

The Ministry of Education recently issued a circular to the education departments of various provinces and cities, instructing provincial and registered private universities to appropriately reduce or exempt tuition fees for students from Shaanxi, Gansu, Suiyuan, and Chahar provinces this year. Recently, it issued another circular to national universities, ordering them to waive all tuition and miscellaneous fees for students from the above-mentioned four provinces this year.

Ministry of Education Orders Restriction on Excessive Spending 90

Before the Budget for the 19th Year is Determined

The Ministry of Education received an order from the Executive Yuan stating that before the budgets of various agencies for the 19th year are approved, they can only spend according to the approved budget amount for the 18th year. All expenditures that exceed the quota without approval will be the responsibility of the cashier officials to compensate. The Ministry of Education issued a special circular to the education departments and schools under its direct jurisdiction, citing Executive Yuan Order No. 3187, which cites National Government Order No. 487 and Central Political Conference Consultation stating: "It is proposed that before the budget for the 19th year is established, the emergency measures and implementation details stipulate that if the budget for the 19th year has not been approved, it should be implemented according to the most recent approved plan. Without the approval of the Central Political Conference, expenditures should not be increased." This is because various agencies can only spend according to the approved budget quota for the 18th year before the budget plan for the 19th year is approved. All expenditures that exceed the quota without approval, regardless of the source of funds, whether it belongs to the agency's revenue or savings, are illegitimate. According to the Audit Law and Accounting Regulations, the cashier officials should be responsible for compensation. In order to be prudent with national currency and eliminate waste, it is proposed to ask the National Government to issue a clear prohibition. Is this appropriate? Please make a public decision." The matter was brought up for discussion at the 241st meeting of this conference this month and was resolved and passed, consulting the National Government for handling. Accordingly, the case was recorded and consulted with the government for reference, and a separate circular was issued to the subordinates for compliance. Etc. By this, it has been proposed to the 91st State Council meeting of this government, and it has been decided to issue a general order for compliance. In addition to the letter and distribution, a joint order is issued to comply with and instruct the subordinates to comply with. This order." Etc. Following this, in addition to the distribution of orders, this urgent order is issued to comply with. This order.

Old System Middle School Graduates 91

Can Enter High School Second Grade

The Ministry of Education, according to the Guangdong Education Department's presentation based on the presentation of Gu Maowei, the principal of the Provincial Ninth Middle School, stated that the graduates of the old system middle school in the school have filed applications to be inserted into the second grade of high school. Football Season Arrives 98

Chinese football teams joining Westerners' associations must be negotiated through the Chinese Physical Education Advancement Association. Chinese football league games will be brought forward. After the Shanghai Westerners' Football Association began registration for this session, several Chinese football teams went to register. The association, because it had not obtained proof from the relevant Shanghai local Chinese sports authorities, was inconvenient to immediately approve, and sent a special letter to the Chinese National Physical Education Association, roughly stating (Chinese football teams joining the Westerners' Association must be certified and recommended by the Advancement Association before they can register, to clarify the boundaries of football jurisdiction), etc. Therefore, the Advancement Association has specially published this news in the newspaper as a public announcement. Football teams wishing to join the Westerners' Association should submit the team name, organization, and affiliated groups in detail to the Chinese National Physical Education Advancement Association on Labor Father Road within the next few days, so that they can negotiate with the Westerners' Association, it is said.

Moreover, the Chinese Football Federation had more than 50 member teams in the last session, with fierce competition and progress in the football skills of each team, which was greatly different from the past. Unfortunately, the competition was suspended for a long time due to the influence of the weather. Some school teams therefore failed to finish the competition. This session plans to advance the start time of the association's competition. Letters have now been sent to all old members to solicit opinions on joining. Because the competition venues are insufficient, the recruitment of new members will depend on the number of old members, it is said.

The Initiation of the Women's Table Tennis League 99

Since the promotion of table tennis in 1918, the skills have been improving day by day. Our country has already occupied a considerable position in the world. In recent years, the world has gradually paid attention to this sport. More than ten teams have been established one after another, but without a unified organization, they cannot progress consistently, making it difficult to achieve the purpose of table tennis, and to abolish improper indoor entertainment. Now, Lin Muzhao and Lin Murong of the Guangdong Women's Table Tennis Team, Li Ruifen and Zhang Runzhu of Liangjiang, and Guo Guangji and Chen Jinju of Patriotic intend to widely recruit like-minded people to organize the Shanghai Women's Table Tennis Federation. Before the establishment, Mr. Yu Binqi, the main organizer of the National Table Tennis Federation, will be in charge of all preparations. Any women's table tennis groups wishing to join the joint organization can send a letter to Mr. Yu at Xinli, 6 Jiujiang Road, it is said.

Hong Kong Chinese Football Team Loses One and Wins One in Singapore 102

丨Lost the first game 1-2 to the Singapore League, Won the second game 3-2丨

(Singapore Dispatch, August 27) The Hong Kong Chinese Football Team came south to try its voice, and met its strong opponent, the Singapore League. In the first battle on August 25, the tiger fell in Pingyang and was bullied by dogs, losing 1-2 to the Singapore League. The second meeting on the 26th, the Singapore League drooped its head and retreated three houses, and was defeated by the Chinese 3-2. The wins and losses are equal. The Chinese team and the Singapore League can be said to be a pair of difficult brothers. The two battles are as follows:

(1) The Chinese Team Tries the Singapore League for the First Time 103

Result: Lost 1-2

The 24th was the day when the Hong Kong Chinese Football Team came south to try its voice for the first time. The team's (tiger) nickname has long been shocking. The people of the South are looking forward to the (tiger)'s stunts. However, the other side, the Singapore League, its players are all contemporary talents. The Singapore League has Ya Jiu (Chinese) in the back defense (one man guards the gate), and Malaysia's God of Feet and God of Head in the front. The Chinese expedition football team encountered them last time, and also painfully lost three goals. Its power can be seen from this. Now that the Chinese team has just raised its flag, it has met this strong enemy. Therefore, the people who are looking forward to the Tiger Gate are especially lively. Around the stadium, there is almost no place to stand. After 2:00 p.m. yesterday, it rained for a long time. Those who care about this battle were all discouraged. Fortunately, it cleared up immediately, and the sunshine shone. The spectators who kept coming on the road before the game all rejoiced, hurrying and bustling, for fear of being late. When the fierce battle was on, it rained again. Most of the spectators stood in the open air, and their clothes and shoes were all wet. Some used paper as umbrellas to avoid the rain temporarily. The athletes' performance in the rain was even more deeply imprinted in our minds. The reporter drove to the venue at 4:10 p.m., but saw several members of the Tiger team in Anshun Law, with a tide of people rising and falling, and the field was full of murderous atmosphere. When approaching the venue gate, he caught a glimpse of several members of the Tiger team riding in Mr. Hu Wenhu's Tiger car, with flags flying on the car, which was extremely spectacular. After arriving, he met Mr. Ye Jiugao, the leader of the Chinese team, and inquired that Mr. Cao Guicheng could not attend due to illness, and Li Hongqing replaced him. Mr. Chen Guangyao arrived as scheduled. The lineups of the two teams are as follows:

Chinese Team

Chen Guangyao

Li Yuda A Zuoxian Sun Jinshun

Chen Xipei Huang Ruihua Huang Bosong

Liang Yutang Li Guizhao He Jiaqiang

Li Hongqing

Singapore League Team

Ya Jiu (Chinese) Yu Shu (Chinese) Ding Niushi (Jiang)

Rui Lao (English) Min Hong (Chinese)

Luo Huada (Malay)

Nu Li De (English) Du La (Malay)

Mo Nu (Malay)

Ya Yao (Chinese) Kun An (Chinese)

The situation is very critical At 4:50, the Chinese athletes, led by captain Li Yuda, rushed out of the crowd. The team members wore yellow shirts, black sleeves, and white pants, running into the field. At first glance, they looked like a group of yellow-spotted tigers. The audience quickly applauded. Then the Singapore League team followed, wearing blue shirts and white pants, full of energy. The notary, Mr. Hua Weilu, then summoned the representatives of the two teams to determine the venue. Then the athletes of the two teams gathered to take pictures. The photographers were very active. After the photos were taken, the Chinese team shouted slogans, and the momentum was strengthened. The battle period had arrived, and the killing opportunity was opened. At this time, the weather was clear after the rain, the scenery was washed, and a rainbow curved in the middle of the sky, colorful and beautiful. Not five minutes after the start, the Chinese forward led the ball straight up, and with one kick, the ball went to the goal, and the situation was very critical. Fortunately, Ya Jiu calmly waved his hand, and the ball went away like an arrow. Before long, drizzle floated, and the open-air audience was discouraged.

Did Not Hit The Target Afterwards, the Malay forward of the Singapore League doubled his efforts. Kun An and Min Hong worked together to the best of their ability. The ball was mostly in front of the Chinese goal, and there were two dangers, which were rescued by Chen Xipei. The performance of the two athletes was excellent, and the audience was overjoyed. When the first half was about to end, the Chinese team was penalized with a free kick, which was kicked by Duan Lao. The ball was blocked by a Chinese team member as soon as it was kicked. It did not hit the target. Suddenly, the notary's silver horn sounded, ending the first half without a winner.

Reorganize the Flagship After the five-minute lemon time passed, the two teams changed venues, and the war machine started again. The ball hovered in front of the Chinese goal, and Tuo La and Luo Huada often dribbled the ball straight up. Mo Nao intercepted it, and was about to shoot directly at the goal when the silver horn suddenly sounded. Although the ball penetrated the Chinese goal, it was too late. It was a pity to kick in the air. When the battle reached 5:50, the ball was passed from the Chinese midfielder to the forward Sun Jinshun, who raised his foot and shot. Ya Jiu saw that the ball was in danger and had already deployed a defense. When the ball came, he gently caught it and kicked it away with his foot, turning danger into safety. The two sides fought for about 50 minutes, and they had not yet won or lost. The audience thought that the Chinese team was so brave, and that the battle that day would probably not be won or lost.

Like Losing the Pot Unexpectedly, at 52 minutes, Min Hong of the Singapore League dribbled the ball into the enemy's formation and passed it to Luo Huada. After Luo got the ball, he shot at the enemy's goal, and it went into the net as if he had lost the pot. The Chinese team lost the first goal. When the battle reached 6:00, Huang Bosong got the ball and was pushed out of bounds by Yu Shu. However, Yu Shu was penalized for this foul, and was penalized with a twelve-yard ball, which was stepped on by Sun Jinshun. At this time, Ya Jiu was alone in guarding the empty goal, lonely. Sun chose the price tag and stepped on it. The ball became incurable. The sound of firecrackers rose sharply, celebrating the Chinese team's recovery of a goal. The cheers of the audience resounded far and wide. The Chinese team's popularity is so great.

Two to One At this time, it was already a tie with one to one, and there were only five minutes left. If the Chinese team persisted, both sides would kiss the god of peace. However, things in the world are not necessarily satisfactory. Two minutes before the end, the Chinese team was again attacked by Tuo La of the Singapore League, making it two to one. Although the Chinese team wanted to counterattack, time did not wait for me. At 6:10, a long whistle sounded, and the audience swarmed up, arousing the war, which came to an end. So two to one, the Chinese team announced its defeat.

The performance is very good Watching the battle, the performance of the Chinese team members was very good. Its strength seems to be above the expedition team. Unfortunately, Cao (Xingcheng) and Wu (Jinquan) were ill and could not be on the field. The forward lacked a flying general, which was inevitably a bit weak. Sun Jinshun also seemed to be like Li Huitang's battle, and did not like to chase and win the ball, so it was difficult to win yesterday. If it were not for a twelve-yard ball, then the Chinese team would have suffered the same bad luck as the expedition team. Fortunately, the internal guard is strong, especially Liang Yutang is pleasing to the eye, and is highly praised by the audience. Even without Wu Jinquan, his strength is not weakened.

(2) Won the Singapore League Again 104

Result: Three to Two

The Hong Kong Chinese Football Team made its second expedition on the 27th. The opponent was originally the Western League, but due to other reasons, it was changed to the Singapore League, so its lineup has changed slightly. Wanren, the leader of the Chinese team, has also joined the battle. The Chinese team, however, because Chen Cao has gone to Medan, the left and right wings have to be replaced by Mai and Li. Center forward Huang Bosong was injured in the waist in the previous battle and has not yet recovered, so he was unable to play. Therefore, the center forward who responded to the battle yesterday has been changed to He Jiaqiang, and He's internal auxiliary position has been filled by Liang Rongda. Yesterday, after the formation was set, a group of Chinese spectators were very worried about the Chinese team, thinking that Chen Cao's departure was like breaking an arm, and now with Huang's absence, the situation would be weaker than the previous forward. However, the result was the opposite. Yesterday's performance was not only better than before, but also defeated the Singapore League by three to two, recovering the lost reputation.

Deadlocked When the war started, the ball flew back and forth, and the direction was uncertain. People also ran back and forth, and both offense and defense were strong. The two armies were deadlocked and refused to give in to each other. The Chinese team lost many opportunities due to the weakness of the left wing. They could not intercept the ball, and their attacks were not accurate. As a result, several balls in front of the goal were lost in an instant. After sighing, people remembered Cao and Chen, thinking that if there were flying generals and train heads, there would not be such a loss. Wanren, who was expected by thousands of people to be able to do so, was slightly slow in action due to his large body, but his dribbling and fighting for the ball still had unique advantages that no one could match.

The Pillar of a Team He Jiaqiang deserves to be the pillar of a team. In the battle that day, his performance was particularly good. Of the three goals won by the Chinese team, in addition to one goal because the Singapore League's goal was in danger, the goalkeeper was unable to save the ball when he fell to the ground, and the defender hurriedly stepped the ball into his own net with one foot, the rest were all scored by He. The first goal was kicked in in the tenth minute of the first half, and the second goal was passed from the right wing to the front of the goal in the fiftieth minute of the second half, and was headed in by He Jiaqiang. His posture when heading the ball was like a wild child turning over, which was especially applauded by the audience. However, in addition to scoring three goals, the Chinese team had no room for further progress.

Good Liaison The Singapore League, on the other hand, fought hard from beginning to end. Its forward's charge into the battle was unusually brave. Dribbling and intercepting the ball were beyond the reach of the Chinese team, and the liaison was particularly good. Therefore, although the first half ended with a score of zero to one, the second half was still able to tie with two to two. If it were not for the self-inflicted mistake of defender Wilson, it would not have been declared a defeat.

Yesterday's 99 Commemoration Meeting 105

Commemoration of the Premier's First Uprising

A Total of More Than Nine Hundred Representatives Attended

Yesterday was the anniversary of the Premier's first uprising. The Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters Propaganda Department specifically designated the morning of that day at 9:00 a.m. to hold a commemoration meeting at the Republic Cinema on Minquan Road. Prior notice was given to all levels of party headquarters, agencies, groups, and schools in the city, requiring them to send four representatives to attend the meeting. A total of more than nine hundred representatives attended the meeting. The meeting was chaired by Yang Qingyuan, Minister of the City Propaganda Department. After reporting on the knowledge and efforts that should be made in the 99 Commemoration, Tong Xingbai, Hou Dachun, and others gave successive speeches, and finally slogans were shouted. The meeting then adjourned. Details are recorded below:

Meeting Order (1) All stand at attention, (2) Sing the Party Song, (3) Give the highest salute to the Party and National Flag and the Premier's Portrait, (4) Chairman respectfully reads the Premier's Will, (5) Observe three minutes of silence to mourn the martyrs, (6) Chairman's report, (7) Speeches, (8) Slogans, (9) Adjournment.

Meeting Staff (Chairman) Yang Qingyuan, (Recorder) Zhou Hanmei, (Master of Ceremonies) Xu Yefu, (Reception) Cao Huaqiu, Li Wenhuan, Chen Ming, Jiang Zhenwu, (Officers) Hong Dichan, Yang Shaozhi, Zhang Hanyun.

Returned to the Philippines on the Original Ship Last Night

The Results of the Petition Are Still Satisfactory

Mr. and Mrs. Roxas, Speaker of the Philippine House of Representatives, arrived in Shanghai at 9:00 yesterday morning aboard the President Jackson from America and returned to the Philippines on the same ship at 12:00 last night. Those who went to the pier to welcome them included Chen Shiguang and Liu Yunfang from the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, as well as many of Roxas' relatives and friends in Shanghai. Traveling Companions: Accompanying Mr. and Mrs. Roxas on their return to the Philippines were Roxas' cousin, Mrs. Osea, Mr. Lee Ke Ko, Secretary of the Philippine Independence Petition Group, Miss Gifford, and Roxas' secretary, Fuentes, a total of six people.

According to Roxas, Quezon's health has been improving daily. The Public Concession

Reactions to the Increased Water Rates 109

The Opinion of the Municipal Authorities

The Shanghai Waterworks Company of the Public Concession, citing the increased price of bids and the increased costs, which made it impossible to pay dividends to shareholders, reported to the Public Works Department for approval to increase water rates by 25 percent. Since the publication of this news in various newspapers, it has aroused a reaction from the general residents of the concession. Recently, the Fourth District Party Department of this city believes that tap water is one of the public utilities, and the livelihood of the entire people should be considered, and it should not be solely for the purpose of profit. The company previously increased the water rate standard from 10 percent to 22 percent, and the burden on the citizens has already felt too heavy. The rent of houses has increased this year, and the company's income has also increased invisibly. Even if it is affected by the high price of gold and low price of silver, how can it not save expenses to make up for the deficit? Why should it only exploit the people's livelihood and increase water rates again? It was submitted by the Municipal Executive Committee and transferred to the Municipal Government for negotiation and prohibition. The Municipal Government then sent it to the Public Utilities Bureau for verification. It is heard that the Bureau believes that the business of the Shanghai Waterworks Company is entirely in the concession. The places where water is supplied across the border are now being negotiated for recovery in order to reduce water prices and make them consistent with those in Shanghai South and Zhabei. Fortunately, although water prices in the concession have increased, water prices in the Chinese area remain the same, which is cheaper than the concession. The difference is even greater now. Citizens of the concession can move to the Chinese area, enjoy cheap water, and revitalize the Chinese area. Therefore, the Municipal Party Department is requested to actively advocate and persuade them, and at the same time send letters to Yuan Ludeng and Yu Qiaqing, who are Chinese directors of the Public Works Department of the Public Concession, to quickly find ways to provide relief and alleviate the people's difficulties.

Real Estate Association

Protest Against Increased Water Rates 110

Increasing Water Rates Due to Sharp Drop in Exchange Rate... Why Didn't They Reduce Prices Before? The Company's Largest Expenditure is Raw Materials... The Yangtze River's Flow of the Huangpu River

The Shanghai Real Estate Association yesterday submitted a serious letter of protest to the Shanghai Waterworks Company. The full text is translated as follows: This is a formal protest against the increase of the tap water surcharge by 25 percent, which will be collected during the appropriate period. The Association believes that the statement issued by your company on August 6 in various newspapers, explaining the reasons for the increase of the tap water surcharge and the process, is unreasonable. Increasing water prices is not allowed in principle, and it should not be regarded as a temporary expedient. If it is implemented, it will violate the contract signed by the Public Works Department and your company on March 17, 1928. Please explain as follows: Although tap water is one of the public utilities, it cannot be equated with other public utilities, because tap water is not only a natural monopoly enterprise, but the product it supplies is absolutely indispensable to human life. Municipal experts even advocate that tap water must be absolutely undertaken by the public sector, because it is not only because tap water has a close relationship with public health, which can affect the rate of death and disease in a city, but also because private operators are afraid that they will seek profits and damage public interests. Therefore, tap water companies are different from private enterprises. Private enterprises seek high profits for shareholders, while tap water companies must create happiness for society. Their service policy and business policy should be based on social welfare everywhere. If they only seek profit for shareholders and do not hesitate to sacrifice social welfare, it is contrary to the principles of operating public utilities. The proposal of your company to increase the surcharge this time has damaged the interests of the entire society and individual users, which is by no means insignificant. Therefore, it has to be regarded as an unreasonable act, which is difficult for the entire citizens to accept. Although the Public Works Department has approved it, the approval of the public precedes the approval of the authorities. Secondly, the reason why your company proposes to increase prices is that the exchange rate has plummeted, prices have soared, and this year's net profit has therefore suffered losses, and the annual dividends are insufficient to pay. Before, when the exchange rate was high, we have never heard of your company's proposal to reduce prices, and the citizens have not benefited from it. Therefore, the losses caused by the sharp drop in the exchange rate cannot be compensated from the citizens. Moreover, tap water charges have followed the house prices for a long time. At present, due to land prices and construction relations, the price of houses has been more than ten to fifteen times higher compared with 20 years ago, and the water charges have also increased, which is quite alarming. Your company's economic foundation should be very stable. The guarantee money accumulated under the two items of (average dividend) and (revision of price) should be enough to pay this year's dividend, and it must be to increase the water price in order to make up for the deficit. Your company has increased the price by 20 percent in the past three years, and now it is collecting a surcharge of 25 percent, and it is said that it will have to increase it next year, which is really incomprehensible to the Association. As for the rising prices, the largest item in a company's expenditure should be raw materials. The raw material of your company is the continuous flow of the Huangpu River. If it is said that the cost of engineering has increased, the cost of laying water pipes should be a large item in the engineering expenditure. In fact, the water pipes in the houses everywhere are installed by the owners, and the cost of connecting to the main water pipe is still borne by the owners, from 60 taels of silver for a quarter of an inch pipe to 175 taels of silver for a four-inch pipe. Therefore, the cost of engineering for your company is actually borne by the owners for a part of it. Judging from the source of raw materials and the cost of engineering, the so-called rising prices are not enough to be a reason for increasing the surcharge. Finally, there is one more thing to say, that your company's increase in water prices violates the contract of March 17, 1928, because the contract stipulates a price, and the price cannot be changed during the effective period of the price rate. If it is said that the increase of the surcharge is to reduce the increase of the price rate next year, whether the increase next year is possible and whether it can be implemented still depends on the social assessment and approval. How can it be used as a reason for the current increase of the surcharge? Moreover, the Public Works Department once said that if the exchange rate returns to two shillings, this issue will be reconsidered. At the moment, the exchange rate has gradually increased, and the so-called increase next year may be only possible. This Association is composed of the Shanghai real estate industry. The submission of this protest is not only on behalf of the will of the members of this Association, but also on behalf of the public opinion of all residents, because the residents are deeply affected by the increase in water prices, and it is not only the members of this Association, etc. According to Mr. Li Bohan, the secretary of the Association, the letter to the Public Works Department has also been drafted and will be published in the near future.

The Maritime Industry is Declining in China

Japanese Ships Are Uniquely Prosperous in Chinese Shipping 116

Japanese ships to China have always held the principle of gaining an inch and wanting a mile. Since China and Japan revised the new treaty and our country has been working hard to recover inland and coastal navigation rights, the Japanese side has still used diplomatic means to maintain the current status of shipping. However, in terms of business and navigation rights, they are constantly making progress. However, the Daishengchang Company, a small wheel company in the inland rivers of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, was automatically abandoned by the Japanese because they had already made huge profits. The main reason was that there were many ships and the business was slow, and there were occasional dangers on the way. Therefore, it was transferred to the Chinese to take over. If it is the Yangtze River or the coastal routes, the number of Japanese ships has increased rather than decreased. In the first six months of this year, the number of Japanese ships entering and leaving the port has increased by more than 400 compared with last year. This is clear evidence. The latest news on the Japanese shipping industry's progress in China is as follows:

Coastal Ships Expand Routes: Among the Sino-Japanese shipping routes, the Nippon Yusen Kaisha's (NYK) business is uniquely large. In recent years, since the long-distance and coastal shipping have been divided into two companies, operating independently of each other, the company's Japan-Yangtze River route has been transferred to the management of the coastal company. On this route, 9 to 11 regular ships have been designated. The main purpose of its business is to transport steel from Daye, fresh eggs from Anhui, and rapeseed from Wuhu. At the same time, Eastern goods are directly transported to various ports along the Yangtze River. This year, the Japanese shipping industry is also in a downturn, and the number of ships停泊 is increasing. In order to adjust transportation and prevent ships from being empty, the coastal company has planned to open a new route in the ports of North and South China, preparing to use six ships to operate first, three in South China and three in North China. It has submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications for subsidies. It is confirmed that this case has been approved by the Japanese government, and the company is planning to implement it. The Dalian Shipping Company's new South China route can also be opened within the year.

The Number of Japanese Coal Ships is Gradually Decreasing: There are many Japanese "wild chicken" ships operating in Shanghai and the Yangtze River. These ships mostly carry Japanese coal to China. In the first six months of this year, a total of 430,000 tons of Japanese coal arrived in Shanghai, a decrease of 180,000 tons compared with the same period last year. The number of Japanese coal-carrying "wild chicken" ships has also decreased in Shanghai. The reason is the influence of rising gold prices. However, the regular ships between China and Japan have increased rather than decreased in the past two months because Japanese yarn, cloth, white sugar, rubber appliances, silk fabrics, and洋紙 are crowded to be transported to China.

Nissin's Yangtze River Shipping Business is the Best: The number of Shanghai's Yangtze River ships has increased from three companies to six. This year, due to the situation, Chinese Yangtze River ships have been suspended for a long time. Among the foreign ships on the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River, the business of Taikoo and Jardine is not as good as that of Nissin. According to recent months, Nissin accounts for the first place in the Yangtze River export cargo of the three foreign ships, Taikoo second, and Jardine third. According to the Shanghai Yangtze River cargo, the first is cloth and cotton yarn, and the second is white sugar, cigarettes, kelp, and foreign groceries. These have a larger income from water foot, while ironware, salt, and matches are the worst. In the past six months, the yarn, sugar, tobacco, seafood, and paper loaded by Nissin have been twice as much as Taikoo and 70-80% more than Jardine. Even the miscellaneous sugar in the incoming cargo is better than the British. This time, the Xiang rice transported to Shanghai is mostly carried by Nissin ships.

Liaison Ships are Packed with Passengers: The Shanghai Maru and Nagasaki Maru, the NYK's liaison fast ships, have been crowded with passengers in recent months. The main reason is that the Shanghai summer resort guests who went to Lushan and Guling in previous years could not go this year due to banditry. Most people changed their plans to go to Unzen and other places in Japan. The cabins of all levels were all booked up. The crackdown on Chinese people going to Japan is strict. If there is no entry and exit permit issued by the Japanese Marine Police Department, the ticket will still be refused.

It was passed. The proposer was immediately nominated to draft the declaration. The China State-Produced United Commercial Center has been open for two months, and the business situation is still stable. The latest news on the Japanese shipping industry's progress in China is as follows:

Reasons for Shortages in Public Weight Inspection of Raw Silk 121

Letter from the Commodity Inspection Bureau to the Silk Factory Guild

To the Shanghai Silk Factory Guild Committee:

According to reports from member silk factories, since the Raw Silk Inspection Office implemented public weight inspection on a trial basis, the silk factories have suffered significant losses due to shortages. We have specifically written to the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau to request an explanation of the reasons for these shortages and how to improve the situation. The original letter was published in this newspaper on the 30th of last month. After receiving the letter, the Bureau immediately instructed the Raw Silk Inspection Office to review it and provide a response. They have now sent a detailed response to the Guild, explaining the matter thoroughly for distribution to all members. The original letter is transcribed below:

Response:

We have received your Guild's letter, which stated (original letter omitted as it was published in the previous issue) etc. We immediately instructed the Raw Silk Inspection Office to review the matter and provide a response. According to their response, the Shanghai Silk Factory Guild's letter raises approximately four points: (1) Agreement on the implementation of the public weight system to maintain fairness in transactions; (2) Request for an explanation of the causes of shortages; (3) Dissatisfaction expressed regarding shortages observed even in the most water-sufficient and dry silk from the Xinchang Silk Factory; (4) Request for research and improvement of public weight inspection methods. The office has carefully reviewed the matter. It is noted that when public weight inspection of raw silk was first implemented, some silk merchants were deeply suspicious. Now, according to the Guild's letter, the silk factories all acknowledge that the implementation of the public weight system can maintain fairness in transactions, strengthening trust in foreign trade. This progress in the thinking of the silk factories, in line with global trends, is a cause for great celebration for the future of China's silk industry. Raw silk, by its nature, is soft and readily absorbs and releases moisture. If the humidity is high or the water content is insufficient, the moisture content will be high and the buyer will suffer losses. If the humidity is low or the water content is sufficient, the seller will feel disadvantaged. European countries, after decades of research and experimentation, determined in 1840 that raw silk should contain 9.91% moisture. At the same time, they also established a method for determining the public weight. First, the total net weight is determined. Next, the total moisture content is determined. Then, the total dry weight is calculated. Finally, 11% is added to the dry weight to arrive at the public weight. This method has been deemed appropriate by various countries and has been used for 90 years. Since raw silk should contain 9.91% moisture, if the silk released by various factories contains more than 9.91% moisture, the public weight will be less than the net weight. If it contains less than 9.91% moisture, the public weight will be more than the net weight. In recent months, the public weight of the silk from most factories has been less than the net weight. The reason for this is that the silk released by the factories contains more than 9.91% moisture. According to the office's research, the reasons for such high moisture content are approximately fivefold: (1) Insufficient water content; (2) Old and worn-out reeling machines that cannot maintain heat; (3) Excessive distance between the reeling room and the silk room. When the silk is dropped, it is easily absorbs moisture. The silk room or silk box may not have adequate water content or may not be humidified, causing the silk from the reeling room to absorb excessive moisture. (4) Export merchants' silk warehouses may be located on the first floor, or on the second or third floors. The air temperature is lower in the upper levels. If the raw silk is stored on the lower levels for three days, the phenomenon of excessive moisture absorption will be particularly evident. (5) Humid weather. If any one of these factors is present, the moisture content of the raw silk will be high, and a shortage will be found during inspection. If several factors are present, the moisture content will be even higher, and the shortage will be even more pronounced. The office inspects raw silk according to internationally recognized scientific methods. The results of the inspection, whether there is a shortage or not, depend on the moisture content of the silk. Technicians cannot manipulate the results or hold preconceived notions that the silk from a particular factory must be inferior or that the silk from another factory must be superior. The attitude of impartiality is maintained when inspecting raw silk from all factories, regardless of the manufacturer, using the same procedures. Therefore, in the past six months, the results of the office's public weight inspection have been consistent with those of the New York Raw Silk Certification Bureau in the United States. If the silk from a certain factory is expected to be superior and a shortage is found, or if the silk is not expected to have a shortage but one is found, not only will foreigners be unconvinced and international trade will be undermined, but the silk factory guild members will also accuse the office of being biased and will be critical of it. While Xinchang may believe its silk to be the most water-sufficient and dry, the office cannot hold such a preconceived notion and must rely solely on the results of the inspection. The pursuit of scientific advancement is endless, and the office has always emphasized the importance of research and improvement. Since its establishment, the public weight inspection has gained international credibility, and the office has begun researching raw silk grading. Now that the Guild members not only express confidence in the adoption of the public weight system but also hope to improve the current method of determining public weight, their high expectations are commendable. However, this method took decades for Europeans and Americans to develop and has been used for 90 years without any perceived flaws. It is unrealistic to expect the office to invent a better method than the current public weight inspection method in a short period of time to fulfill the silk merchants' great wishes. Given China's lagging scientific development, it is indeed not easy to achieve such results in a short period of time. We will keep this goal in mind for the future. As for the application of the public weight inspection method, 40 new Swiss silk drying machines were purchased and meticulously arranged when the office was established, in order to achieve inspection results comparable to those of Western and Eastern countries. In the past few months, we have dared not be complacent and have worked diligently at all times. The weight and accessories of each silk drying machine have been constantly checked and calibrated. The weight before and after drying is carefully checked by a second person. All those who have visited the office are aware of this. The technicians work conscientiously and are fully responsible. As instructed, we have prepared this written response with the results of our review and sent it to the Guild. We hope that you will distribute it to all members for their information.

Urgent Telegram for Relief after the Chongqing Fire 123

The Chongqing General Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to Shanghai stating (details omitted): A great disaster has befallen us, resulting in a catastrophe. On the [Eighth month] day of this month (August), a fire broke out outside Chuqimen in Chongqing due to negligence. The fire quickly spread throughout the city and divided into multiple directions, reaching Sanpaifang in the north, Daliangzi in the west, Jinzimen outside the city in the south, Jinzijian above, and Taipingmen below, turning everything into scorched earth. The outskirts were densely populated by the poor, while the city center was the commercial hub with numerous warehouses. The fire was finally extinguished at 10 PM, covering an area of several miles and affecting over 10,000 households. The victims were charred and distraught, their cries shaking the heavens. This is an unprecedented tragedy. Our association, witnessing this, is heartbroken. In addition to immediately dispatching various fire brigades to do their best to extinguish the fire, we conducted a post-disaster survey and found endless debris and countless victims scattered everywhere, exposed to the elements and desperately in need of food. We are currently organizing emergency relief to provide temporary assistance, but the disaster area is too large and the need for relief is overwhelming. Chongqing is impoverished and is already recovering from a severe drought this year. Now, it has suffered this devastating blow. Therefore, we urgently appeal to officials at all levels, as well as various organizations, legal entities, prominent merchants, and charitable individuals, to recognize the severity of the disaster and provide generous assistance. This will not only benefit the tens of thousands of victims but also deeply appreciated by the entire population of Chongqing. We respectfully submit this telegram, hoping for your consideration. All staff members of the Chongqing General Chamber of Commerce bow in gratitude.

本埠新聞二 (Local News II)

Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Prepares Ningbo Tide-Watching Special Train 127

The Qiantang River tidal bore is at its most magnificent during the ninth year of the Republic [1920]. The waves reached the seventh level of the Zhenhai Pagoda. In the ten years since then, the waves have not exceeded two zhang [~6.6 meters] at most, which those who have grown accustomed to it don't find strange. This year, due to weather conditions, the tidal bore is quite large. The so-called "ghost tide" during this month has already sounded like thunder, and the night tide is even more intense. Residents are awakened from their dreams and brave the rain and wind to watch, day and night. It is expected that the tidal bore during the eighth lunar month will be even greater than in the ninth year of the Republic. As a result, the business of hotels and temporary shops in Ningbo and the seawall area is exceptionally prosperous. The Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway always runs a special tide-watching train for three days in mid-August on the lunar calendar and prepares tide-watching areas along the Qiantang River in Haining. This year's tidal bore is more magnificent than usual, and the Railway Administration is actively preparing a special train and a riverside viewing area to ensure that tide-watching travelers are not disappointed.
