Thief apprehended in Tianjin 128

Court Has Dispatched Staff to Tianjin for Extradition

The robbery of 100,000 yuan in banknotes from the Zhejiang Provincial Bank has been repeatedly reported in the newspapers. The police learned from the arrested robbers that there were four other perpetrators present at the scene, named Zhu, Ma, Su, and Hu. Ma grabbed the handbag, and Zhu fired the gun. However, they all fled to Tianjin, so the police immediately telegraphed military police agencies in Tianjin, requesting them to be vigilant when ships from Shanghai arrive. The police recently received a telegram from Tianjin stating that Zhu Dexin, the thief who fired the gun, has been apprehended and requested that staff be dispatched to Tianjin for extradition. They then requested the Special District Court to prepare the necessary documents and send detectives to Tianjin. It is expected that the thief will be brought back to Shanghai in four or five days. Ma, Hu, and Su are also being vigorously pursued. He is expected to arrive in Shanghai on Friday and will be handed over to the Special District Court for questioning on Saturday. According to the accomplice detained at the Old Gate Police Station, Zhu was the one who initiated the robbery of the Zhejiang Provincial Bank's funds and fired the gun. In addition, Ma, Wu, and Su are also major suspects in the case and are currently being pursued by the police.

Numbers Three and Four

City Ferryboats Launched the other day 129

In order to develop water transportation and facilitate the travel of citizens on both sides of the Huangpu River, the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau ordered two high-speed large ferryboats last year to operate between the Bund of Nanjing Road in Puxi and the Donggou area of the Qingning Market in Pudong. The cost was ten times higher than that of other small steamers, but the fares remained at the same level as ten years ago, so everyone considered the prices to be low, the ride to be smooth and comfortable. However, the citizens of Gaoqiao felt regret that the new ferryboats could not reach their area, which is not far from Donggou. Therefore, the municipal government instructed the Public Utilities Bureau to actively prepare for extending the line to Gaoqiao. After receiving the order, the bureau contracted with the Hexing Factory on June 10th of this year to build the third and fourth ferryboats for use in Gaoqiao. Each boat cost approximately 70,000 taels, including the engine. Each boat is 108 feet long, 20 feet wide, 8 feet 6 inches high, and has a draft of 5 feet, a horsepower of 200, and a capacity of 600 passengers, with a speed of 11 knots. Compared to the original numbers one and two ferryboats, the equipment and layout have been further improved and perfected, and the latest artistic ideas have been incorporated, such as the electric lights, door latches, and switches, which were all ordered from famous German factories and are exquisite and durable. After the contract was signed, the Hexing Factory actively built the boats and launched them at 2:30 PM on September 8th. Representatives from the municipal government, the manager of the Municipal Bank, and the director and technicians of the secretariat of the bureau all visited the boats and were satisfied with the construction and launching. In order to avoid unnecessary formalities, the bureau did not have a bottle-breaking ceremony or other rituals. The factory explained to the Public Utilities Bureau that, based on decades of experience, they voluntarily enlarged and widened the materials and dimensions specified in the bureau's specifications and drawings, without requesting an increase in price. This is a rare occurrence in the shipbuilding industry, and their enthusiasm for supporting municipal construction is commendable. The engineer from the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau also visited the boats the other day and considered them to be the most beautiful ferryboats in the East.

Photograph of New City Ferryboats Being Launched (Wang Kai Photography)

Overview of Construction in this City in August 130

In August of this year, the Bureau of Public Works issued permits for a total of 145 construction projects, 217 repair projects, 100 miscellaneous projects, and 28 demolition projects. Compared to the previous month, construction and demolition were roughly the same, while repair and miscellaneous projects each increased by about one-third. Compared to the same month last year, construction was similar, while repair and miscellaneous projects decreased slightly, and demolition increased slightly. The total construction area in the city (excluding rural bungalows) was approximately 3,540 square *fang*, a decrease of over 900 square *fang* compared to the previous month, but still an increase compared to May. The estimated total value was over 1,141,000 yuan, a decrease of over 80,000 yuan compared to the previous month. In terms of area by district, the French Concession south of Shanghai was the highest, followed by Zhabei, then the French Concession west of Shanghai and Yangjing. In terms of estimated value, the French Concession south of Shanghai was the highest, followed by the French Concession west of Shanghai, then Zhabei, and finally Yangjing. The reason for the discrepancy between the ranking of estimated value and area is that there are many large buildings along the roads built beyond the boundaries of the French Concession west of Shanghai, so its estimated value is higher than Zhabei. As for Yangjing, it is mostly bungalows, so it cannot be compared with the French Concession west of Shanghai. Zhabei district, which usually ranks second in terms of area and estimated value, had jumped to first place in May, June, and July of this year, but suddenly decreased this month. There were no particularly large projects this month. In the French Concession west of Shanghai, there were three locations with estimated values of 50,000 to 60,000 yuan each. In the French Concession south of Shanghai, the Yilexin Housing Agency built commercial housing and cement warehouses at Beijixiang Lane, outside of Waitan Road, covering a total area of 250 square *fang*, with a total estimated value of approximately 107,000 yuan. Also, in the Jiangwan district, a Mr. Chen built the Dizang Temple and sacrificial pavilion at the end of Yuexiu Road and Jiangchang Road, covering an area of 210 square *fang*, with an estimated value of approximately 102,000 yuan. As of the end of August, only half of the dangerous buildings that were ordered to be forcibly demolished had actually been demolished.

The Taxpayers' Association Asks the Municipal Government to

Negotiate the Lu Lianqiao Case 131

The Shanghai Chinese Taxpayers' Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Government yesterday, stating: "Respectfully, according to the letter from the Shangyu Association in Shanghai, dated August 19th, this association received a report from Qian Yusun (teacher at Chengzhong School), representative of Lu Lianqiao's son, Lu Bingjun, an employee of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce. The report stated that on the afternoon of the 7th of this month at 5:50 PM, Lu Lianqiao was waiting for a tram at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Shimen Road. At that time, an American, He Mo Li, was driving car number 11578 from west to east at high speed, without honking the horn. As a result, the front wheel of the car hit his father, causing him to fall unconscious beside the tram door. If He had even a little conscience, he would have stopped the car immediately, and it would not have resulted in serious injury and death. However, He continued to drive at high speed, and his father was hit violently by the rear wheel, smashing him against the iron pillar of the tram station, causing severe head injuries. He immediately fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. He, at this point, did not even take his father to the hospital in his car, but drove away. Later, a patrolman sent him to Renji Hospital for treatment, but he died on the morning of the 11th. The Special Court appointed Prosecutor Xu to examine the body, and instructed He to be responsible for compensation, but He refused to comply. (Omission) We beg your association to support us." After discussion by the executive committee of this association, it was decided that the matter concerned the lives of Chinese people and the dignity of the nation, and that the association should represent Lu Bingjun and send a letter to various organizations to seek unanimous support. (Omission) It was handed over to the standing committee for active handling. Therefore, we are writing to request the assistance of the general assembly and to request that your opinions on assistance be communicated to us. We have learned that the American consular jurisdiction in China has not yet been abolished, and our country's laws cannot effectively restrain the murderer in this case. This association believes that the only way is to follow the case of the British soldier beating Zhang Xueliang to death last year, and request your government to negotiate seriously with the American consul in Shanghai in order to achieve the purpose of compensating the victim's family, punishing the murderer, and protecting the lives of the people. Withholding Wages

Dismissal of Chinese and Foreign Staff of the Dredging Bureau 132

Meisheng, the British director of the Zhanghuabang workshop of the Dredging Bureau, was found to have withheld wages from short-term copper workers, failed to provide formal positions to those who had worked for three years, and solicited large bribes. As a result, the workers became suspicious and jointly submitted a petition to the head office, requesting promotions and increased salaries. Song, the director of the Dredging Bureau, found that the wage figures listed in the original petition did not match, and that wages had been withheld by 30 to 50 cents per day. When the director requested leave to return home, the deputies, Chinese nationals Cai Rongfu and Tang Xuanqing, were interrogated by the bureau, and both claimed that it was done by Meisheng. However, as the matter involved suspicion, Cai and Tang were sent to the General Police Station for bail. Meisheng was then summoned back to Shanghai by telegram. After repeated interrogations of the victimized workers from Zhanghuabang at the bureau by the Chinese and foreign directors of the Dredging Bureau, they all testified that the foreign director had withheld wages and solicited large bribes. When asked about this, Meisheng claimed that he had been extremely loyal to his service in the Dredging Bureau and that he had deducted wages and stored them separately to reward diligent workers because the workers were negligent, which led to the slanderous accusation. It is now reported that Director Song and Customs Officer Mei have investigated and determined that, no matter what, the workers' hard-earned wages should not be withheld, and it has been found that wages have been withheld for more than a year, which cannot be denied. This practice must not continue in this bureau, and Director Meisheng should be immediately dismissed. The Chinese nationals Cai Rongfu and others concealed the matter and failed to report it, and should also be dismissed.

Yesterday's Trial in the British Police Court

Indian Constables Accused of Serious Insult Case 133

According to the *Continental News*, Indian constables Meigexin and Luerxin, stationed at 26 and 28 Jiangxi Road, were accused of seriously insulting a Mr. Ni, an employee of a certain inn, on the night of the 6th. The trial opened yesterday (the 8th) in the British Police Court. The police lawyer, Wen De, stated that on that day at midnight, the victim was waiting for a tram on the road when the two defendants approached and dragged him to the building at 26 Jiangxi Road. The victim initially mistook them for street patrolmen, so he went with them. However, upon arriving at the location, they subjected him to indecent behavior and threatened him with a gun. The victim then went out to the road and told a Chinese constable, inviting him to go to 26 Jiangxi Road. One of the two defendants even offered five silver dollars, hoping to bribe him. The constable then reported to the Western police officer Halai at the General Police Station, who arrested them. After the judge questioned the circumstances of the arrest, he adjourned the court and will continue the trial tomorrow.

Establishment of the Pacific News Agency 134

The French Havas News Agency is an international news organization, its importance matching that of the British Reuters News Agency. Its Far East news operations originally cooperated with Reuters and also sent its own reporters to gather news. Since the European War, the focus of world competition has shifted from the Atlantic to the Pacific. Havas News Agency, feeling the needs of the times, took over the existing Pacific News Agency in Vietnam and expanded it, and signed a contract with a Japanese news agency to exchange news. In addition to the original correspondents around the world, it also established correspondents in Vietnam and Japan, and established a general manager in Shanghai to take charge of the overall operation, naming it the Pacific News Agency. The first step is to import world news into China and publicize the true situation of China to the world. The second step is to cooperate with a Chinese news agency and send reporters to important locations in China. As for its news coverage, it will provide detailed reports on all kinds of world political, economic, and financial news that are relevant to the Far East, including the causes and effects, as well as opinions regarding China and Japan. In addition, the movements of Soviet Russia and the Third International are of great importance, and it will clarify what others have not detailed or even researched. Furthermore, it will communicate several times a month on topics such as North America, the Philippines, and Japan, and their opinions and facts regarding China, as well as the true situation in China, to supplement the shortcomings of telegrams. Although the interests of France and China are relatively shallow, its publicity will be more bland, and the Pacific News Agency plans to open up new paths in addition to the methods adopted by news agencies in various countries, which will definitely be beneficial to China. It is now scheduled to begin issuing drafts on September 10.

The boat captain believed that the bandits had been paying attention to this poisonous substance for a long time because of its high value, and planned to rob it. Yihwo Wharf

Recovery of Stolen Cotton Yarn 149

On the 6th of this month, 160 small bales of cotton yarn were stolen from the Jin Shenfu Road warehouse of the Yihwo Cotton Mill. The police were notified to investigate the case. The day before yesterday at noon, detective Jin Yangwu saw the stolen goods placed in front of 48 Guangdong Road, being loaded onto a car. He questioned Cai Yinlong, who hired the car, about the origin of the cotton yarn. A man surnamed Shen came out to mediate and invited Detective Jin to a nearby restaurant for lunch. During the meal, he offered Jin 30 silver dollars, begging him not to pursue the matter. Jin accepted the bribe. After the meal, he still searched the house at 48 Guangdong Road and found 101 more bales of the original stolen cotton yarn in the pavilion room upstairs. He arrested the woman Wang Wu, who lived in the pavilion room, and Cai Yinlong, and detained them separately at the Yangshupu Police Station. Yesterday morning, the men and women were sent to the District Court, where Judge Ge questioned them. The Western deputy supervisor of the Yihwo Cotton Mill stated that after the theft, it was found that the thieves entered through the window and that the cotton yarn found was indeed the stolen goods. Cai Yinlong confessed that there was a Wang Xianji Yarn Store in the house at 48 Guangdong Road and that he was the cook, claiming to know nothing else. Wang Wu confessed that her husband's name was Wang Xianlin and that he did business in cotton yarn. Wang Xianji was established by her husband, and he had invoices for both buying and selling cotton yarn. Wang Xianlin also went to court with a lawyer and stated that the goods found were purchased from Sun Weisheng on Yuezhou Road, a total of 144 bales, each priced at 5.2 silver dollars. Yesterday afternoon, the car was loaded with eight bales of yarn to show samples to the Yitai Company in the French Concession. Judge Ge asked about the bribery and was told he did not know anything about it. He then ordered Wang Xianlin to be detained and Cai and Wang Wu to be released on bail of 100 dollars each pending further questioning.

Shanghai West Robbery Kills a Bandit 151

Xu Fangshi's House in Danger of Being Robbed

At around 11:00 PM the night before last, more than 20 bandits speaking with a Hakka accent suddenly came to the old house of Xu Fangshi, a villager in the 25th district of Qibao Town in Shanghai West. First, one thief, armed with a bamboo pole, climbed over the roof and opened the main gate, allowing the bandits to enter. When Xu's farmhand, Wang A'gou, heard the noise and opened the door to investigate, a bandit wearing a white undershirt, blue cloth pants, a flat top haircut and barefoot, shot Wang twice, causing him to fall to the ground injured. The thief, holding a gun in one hand and a candle in the other, went straight into Xu's bedroom and opened the door. At this time, the owner, Xu Fangshi, had been awakened from his dream. Hearing the gunshots, he knew it was a robbery. Fortunately, Xu had a self-defense rifle, so he loaded the bullets, extinguished the lights, and waited to fire. When the thief approached, Xu aimed accurately in the dark and fired a shot, hitting the thief in a vital spot, killing him instantly. The candle he was holding fell at the thief's feet, causing him to be scorched by the fire. Several other thieves broke into the back door and fired several shots, but did not dare to enter. Xu also fired back. The gunshots echoed loudly and were heard far and wide. The thieves, seeing that the barefoot thief had been shot and killed, were frightened and did not rob any property, but retreated towards Hengtang. Xu did not dare to pursue them. At dawn, he sent Wang A'gou to Shanghai Hospital for treatment and reported to the Public Security Bureau, requesting a strict investigation. After receiving the report, Inspector Zhao Tingzhen immediately led patrol chief Luo Yanjun and patrol officers Yang Xiaoyan and Zhu Songlin to the scene for investigation. In the dead bandit's belt, they found a Browning bullet, one silver dollar, and two small silver coins. On the ground, they found three Mauser bullet casings and two live bullets, as well as four rifle bullet casings. All were taken back to the station, and a written report was submitted to the Songjiang County Public Security Bureau requesting a thorough investigation and arrest of the bandits. He also ordered the local headman to report to the court for examination.

Special Feature

Rationalization of Industry by Cheng Zhenjun 158

A Great Revolution in Economic Thought

Recommendations of the International Economic Conference

New Trends in the Industrial World of Various Countries

The Only Savior of China's Industry

During this trip abroad to inspect construction administration and important construction projects, we spent half a year, traveled through nine countries, visited more than eighty government agencies and more than thirty social organizations in various countries, and visited nearly a hundred major factories and major projects. We obtained a lot of materials and feelings and will gradually select the important ones for publication. Now, at the beginning of our return to the country, we are deeply questioned by relatives, friends, and reporters. Therefore, we will report in advance on an issue that the Chinese government, the industrial world, and the general public should pay attention to. We hope that comrades and compatriots across the country will conduct in-depth research. What is this matter? It is the so-called industrial rationalization. What exactly is industrial rationalization? It cannot be explained clearly in a few words. We will exhaust the source and tell its origin, then the establishment of its term, and then select and translate several well-known definitions so that readers can think about it. The idea of rationalization originated in Germany. After the European War, Germany was in chaos, all industries were declining, communism was rampant, and huge reparations had to be collected and paid, which was even more painful. The whole country was worried and unable to live in peace. The situation was difficult and forced to this point. Therefore, the only way out was to strive for improvement in industry, to make exports more than imports, and to earn money to make up for the losses. Therefore, the philosopher and industrialist W. Rathenau published great proposals and detailed plans, published many books, and repeatedly stated how to transform industry and how to correct ideas. He also drafted an abstract term to summarize it, called Rationalization. As a result, people across the country rushed to buy and read it, and paper in Luoyang was expensive for a time. The government also expressed deep sympathy and adopted it, establishing the National Efficiency Conference Office. It convened more than 6,000 industrial leaders, divided them into several committees, and studied the transformation of economy and industry. The result was excellent. Therefore, all parties cooperated and proceeded according to the plan, and the industry made a major turnaround. Production increased, consumption decreased, and foreign trade gradually improved. This obvious achievement shocked the world and made people gasp. Seeing this, the League of Nations held the World Economic Conference in Geneva in May 1927. The attendees were representatives of employers, workers, and economists. The Industrial Committee of the conference, referring to the rules and regulations of Germany, decided on many proposals, which were also collectively called Rationalization (Rationalisation in English). This proposal is the specific condition of rationalization, which was formally adopted by the plenary session. It is expected that the people of the country will want to know its contents. The provisions are translated as follows: The resolution of the Industrial Committee of the Geneva Economic Conference on May 17, 1927, Rationalization: Now, because the rational organization of production and distribution is one of the important reasons for increasing production, improving labor conditions, and reducing production costs, and because the purpose of this rationalization is also to (1) obtain the maximum efficiency of labor with the least effort; (2) reduce various different styles (those styles are different, and there are no obvious benefits), study manufacturing methods, the use of standard parts and supplements; (3) eliminate the consumption of raw materials and power; (4) simplify the distribution of goods; (5) eliminate unnecessary transportation, excessive financial burdens, and useless intermediaries. In addition, the wise and lasting application of rationalization methods is generally expected to achieve the following things: First, in the social aspect, the standard of living is improved and stability is increased. Second, in the aspect of consumers, prices are reduced, and goods are more suitable for their needs. Third, in the aspect of various producers, there are more and more reliable benefits, which are fairly distributed to them. In addition, the implementation of rationalization must be cautious to prevent the legitimate interests of workers from being damaged, and appropriate measures must be taken so that the problem of unemployment will not hinder the progress of rationalization at the beginning. In addition, rationalization, in the strict sense of its relationship with labor organization, requires the cooperation of employers and the assistance of business agencies, industrial agencies, and scientific experts. Therefore, the International Economic Conference suggests that all governments, public organizations, business agencies, and ordinary people should pay attention to the following matters: First, producers should devote their efforts to the above aspects and especially implement the following three items: (A) Promote and encourage people to study and compare the most efficient methods of rationalization and scientific management, the easiest steps to implement, and their economic and social impact through various methods; (B) Adopt rationalization in industry, agriculture, commerce, and finance, not only in large-scale enterprises, but also in medium and small-sized enterprises, and even handicraftsmen and shopkeepers should use it. The organization and needs of family life may be able to obtain useful information that must be known; (C) Pay special attention to appropriate means to obtain the best, healthiest, and most respected labor employment, such as job selection, training and leadership, the distribution of work and rest, methods of remuneration for giving a part of the benefits when production increases, in short, the conditions of labor and life must be beneficial to the development and consolidation of their personal personality (2) Systematically and internationally standardize raw materials, accessories, and products of universal trade on a national scale, and eliminate obstacles in production and commerce, which occur only in countries that standardize as a policy (3) Implement research on the best methods adopted by various countries for the application of the above principles and the final results obtained on an international scale, that is, take the research already conducted between several countries as a blueprint, and encourage the exchange of knowledge between relevant groups (4) Further publicize in various places to make people aware of the benefits and benefits arising from rationalization and scientific management and to make them aware of the possibility of gradual realization. At that time, the International Economic Conference was greatly hindered by the economic development of various countries during and after the European War and was eager to adopt rationalization to promote production. The basic industries, such as textiles and coal, can also be restored to their original state. At the same time, it also wanted to promote the economic development of various countries with an international attitude, without being biased towards the prosperity of one or several countries. The Industrial Committee also paid attention to several important developments, which are translated together as follows: (A) Physiology and psychology should be used to study the working life of individuals in the family, in agriculture, in commerce, or in industry; (B) Study the activities of groups according to the same disciplines, and pay attention to various issues, such as methods of paying wages, employee bonuses and employee shareholding, labor-management relations, and other methods of cooperation; (C) In order to establish a scientific basis for production technology, efforts should be made to apply natural sciences, chemistry, physics, mineralogy, and mathematics more widely, because these disciplines are closely related to the raw materials and manufacturing methods of industry; (D) With the same disciplinary thinking, try to apply them to ordinary technical problems arising from the management of individual enterprises, such as house layout, transportation, bookkeeping, office methods, planning, daily affairs, markets, etc., commonly known as (material management); (E) Strive to improve the general organization of production and distribution from a national and international perspective, such as eliminating consumption, simplification and standardization, horizontal mergers and vertical mergers, labor-management contracts, government and public organizations' facilities, the behavior of labor-management organizations, mass production and distribution, the prediction of business trends, and statistical research on the world situation, such as the supply of raw materials, labor, markets, transportation, and power. The Industrial Committee summarized such important developments and its resolutions under the term rationalization. Since this term came out, there have been various explanations, many of which are wrong. I have explained its origin in detail above. Now, I will record the two more satisfactory definitions below. The World Economic Conference stipulates that (Industrial rationalization is a technical and organizational method used to obtain the least consumption of labor and raw materials. All scientific organization of labor, standardization of raw materials and products, simplification of manufacturing methods, and improvement of transportation and market systems are included.) The German National Efficiency Conference stipulates that (Industrial rationalization is to seek knowledge and use various methods with an academic and systematic organization to improve the general economic situation. Its purpose is to supply a large number of cheap, high-quality goods and increase the standard of living. This requires the joint efforts of all aspects of society.) From these two definitions, the resolutions of the International Economic Conference, and the important developments noted by its Industrial Committee, we have a considerable understanding of rationalization. However, what we should distinguish most is that rationalization not only tells us to solve various problems in business with scientific methods, but also makes us have a belief that the world's economic life can be managed rationally, and it is needed. This is a major revolution in world economic thought, and we should pay attention to it. Since the development of manufacturing, the principles of economists, the so-called movements of demand and supply, the so-called recurrent cycles of activity and depression, are often regarded as golden rules. It means that more demand means higher prices, higher prices mean more supply, and more supply means lower prices, so they correspond to each other to achieve balance. (To be continued)

A Laughing Matter 159

— Hai Ke

Mother—Child, come over here. Give this Mrs. Wang next door a kiss.

Child—I don't want to. I don't want to.

Mother—Why not?

Child—I'm afraid she'll hit me. Yesterday I saw Father kissing her, and she hit him.

Man—Darling, I won't call you by your nickname anymore. I'll call you "Revenge."

Woman—That name is too strange. But what does it mean?

Man—There's a Western saying, "Revenge is sweet."

A—You said Mr. is the laziest person among his friends. How do you know?

B—Just look at him when he goes to our company. He'll stand in that revolving door without moving, waiting for someone else to push it before he goes in.

Thief (rummaging through a drawer, muttering softly)—Damn it, damn it. Why doesn't this drawer have even a penny?

Host (wakes up in bed, suddenly bursts out laughing)—Hahaha.

Thief—What are you laughing at?

Host—I'm laughing at myself for needing money too. But this drawer never produces any money. I can't find money even in the daytime, but you're groping around blindly at night. Isn't that too ridiculous?

Interesting Anecdotes in the Barefoot Trend 160

— Qiu Shui

The barefoot movement has been recorded in this publication. Some fashionable women in Shanghai have already been walking barefoot on the streets. And in foreign countries, women's bare feet have become a custom. Since the beginning of summer, there is no pretty woman who is not barefoot, which shows how popular bare feet are. Recently, I read several interesting anecdotes about bare feet in Western newspapers. I am eager to translate them to provide readers with a smile.

Barefoot Maid Fired Recently, the Labor Court in Berlin (the Labor Court specializes in handling labor-management disputes) accepted a very interesting case. The plaintiff was a maid. She was hired by the defendant in May to work as a maid in the defendant's home. At that time, a one-year contract was signed. Less than a week ago, she was suddenly dismissed by the defendant. Therefore, she requested relief. The court asked why she was dismissed. The defendant said that because she was often barefoot and did not understand manners, the master dismissed her. The plaintiff protested, saying that the court should pay attention to the current barefoot trend. In the streets and at banquets, which beautiful woman is not barefoot? Don't they all understand etiquette? As a maid, I can't afford socks, so I took advantage of the situation and went barefoot. I was dismissed for this. Isn't it unfair? Also, I help out at the defendant's house, changing clothes every day and keeping very clean. I just didn't wear a pair of socks, and they accused me of wrongdoing, violating the contract. Please, court, make a fair ruling. The judge who heard the case thought it was very reasonable. He said at the time that bare feet are not a vice, and now it is a popular custom. Even he (the judge) sometimes likes to go barefoot. His daughter also often goes barefoot when she goes out. Therefore, bare feet do not violate etiquette, let alone be used as a reason to dismiss a maid. The defendant heard this and thought that he would definitely lose this lawsuit. He immediately stated that he was willing to settle out of court.

Female Actors Find It Difficult to Go on Stage Barefoot Since the trend of women going barefoot has become so popular, female actors in theaters have also learned to be fashionable and go on stage barefoot. Recently, a theater owner in London named Jones suddenly issued a notice prohibiting female actors from going on stage barefoot. Someone asked him the reason for the prohibition. He said that there was no reason, but it was just unsightly to go on stage with bare feet. Women walking on the street with their feet not wearing socks is no problem. But on a high stage where everyone can see, it seems a bit jarring to be barefoot. This boss's announcement is really interesting. Speaking of women's bare feet, according to ordinary people's arguments, there are several benefits. First, it is comfortable, because less a pair of socks is less a layer of restraint. Second, it is economical. A pair of women's silk stockings costs up to twenty-five yuan. Wouldn't not wearing socks save a lot of money? Third, it is innocent. Not wearing socks reveals the original appearance of the feet, which doesn't add a bit of beautiful curves? Fourth, if it's summer, it's cool. But conversely, when winter comes, the matter of bare feet becomes a problem.

Small Recipes 161

— Yang Yixiao

Lotus Root Cake Take several sections of lotus root and grate them into thin strips on a rice basket. If it is salty, add some salt and chopped green onion. If it is sweet, add a little white sugar. Mix it with flour and fry it in a frying pan until both sides are golden brown. It is loose, crispy, and delicious.

Apple Dumplings Cut apples into small pieces and fill them with bean paste or walnut and jujube filling. Wrap a layer of caul fat on the outside, mix well with egg white batter, and fry them in a frying pan to make dumplings. The taste is quite beautiful.

Gorgon Nut Cake Fresh gorgon nuts are peeled, placed in a stone mortar, and pounded with a pestle. Mix with powdered rock candy and cook into a cake on the pot. It is sweet and delicious.

Anecdotes from the North Station 162

— Lanxi

After our noble countrymen are born for a month, their parents carefully give them a special name. If this special name does not encounter any changes in their lives—damage to their reputation, frustration on the political stage, or even being wanted—they are not willing to change it. Many inexplicable parents call their children cats, dogs, A Mao, A Pig, or those unbearably vulgar names such as A Jin, A Yin, A Bao, A Yu. There are countless other people with the same name. The former Foreign Minister had a Chen Youren, but there is also a Chen Youren in the Translation Section of the Railway Bureau. Because the service agencies are different, they are irrelevant, so there is no need for you to change or me to change. However, interestingly, ten pairs have been found among the two-way staff, with each two people sharing the exact same honorific name and surname. For example, the staff member of the section chief's office in the central section of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway and the person in charge of the two-way resident's vehicle affairs have the same name (Chen Yongqing). The luggage attendant and the Nanjing telegrapher have the same name (Wang Xixian). The servant Wu A'er in the general affairs section and the station attendant at Benniu Station are the same. The roadman Zhou Rongsheng in Zhang Huabang and the luggage clerk at Changzhou Station are the same. The roadman Liu Er in Nanjing and the station attendant at Nanjing Jiangbian Station are the same. After this was discovered, the Management Bureau felt it was inconvenient and has now ordered five people to change their names to avoid confusion.

In this regard, we should acknowledge the Management Bureau's meticulousness and care. But I still have to nag these five people. When changing their names, be sure to carefully flip through the staff directory. Don't learn (avoiding the wind and avoiding the snow). The name that is changed cannot (be the same as others). Thousands of colleagues have high expectations here.

Commentary on Two Famous Roles in the Beikai Records 163

— Danping Shizhu

In recent years, the talents of net roles have become increasingly scarce. The Tongchui (copper hammer) role has even been lamented as difficult to find talent. The framed painted face is relatively broad, but there are not many good materials to be found. Broadly speaking, two people can be obtained from the northern and southern pear garden lines. Who are these two? They are Jin Shaoshan in the south and Hao Shuchen in the north. Hao is the direct disciple of the late famous net Huang San. He has a strong spirit and full of heart and soul. He concentrates on acting and does not slack off at all. Therefore, each play has its own highlights and its own characteristics. He has enjoyed a great reputation for more than ten years and has never suffered any setbacks. Now, he is becoming more and more successful and has a tendency to take the lead in the net role. Shaoshan is the son of Jin Xiushan, the master of the net role. He has specialized in framing since he was a child. Recently, he has also been willing to concentrate on learning the copper clock. Such as Exploring Yin Mountain, Black Wind Scarf, Breaking the Empress Dowager, Going to Heaven Terrace, and Entering the Palace Twice, his singing is meaningful and has the style of his father. The source is from the same vein, and it is better than others. The Beikai Record Company was established the year before last and has invited almost all the famous actors from the north and south to record. Shouchen and Shaoshan are of course also in the net. Shouchen is eccentric in nature and originally had the idea of not recording. Later, after repeated persuasion from friends, he agreed to make an exception to try. When the record was released, Shouchen opened it and listened to it, and suddenly slapped the table and shouted, "If I had known there would be such a result, what harm would it be to record it?" Hearing Shouchen's words, we can know the superb technology of the Beikai engineers. Shouchen recorded a total of four records: One is Loyalty and Filial Piety, One is Beating the Dragon Shed and Beating Cao Bao, One is Eliminating Three Evils, and One is Night Trial of Pan Hong. The Trial of Pan is a Erhuang play, with the thickest rhyme. The first three are pieces with singing and reading, and are particularly vivid and varied. Shuangda is a piece with Erhuang and Xipi, which is more appropriate to match, so the hobbyists are particularly numerous. In addition to Shaoshan's collaboration with Tan Xiaopei and Fu Ying's father and son to record the complete (Catching and Releasing) (Searching for the Orphan and Saving the Orphan), he also recorded four records: (Farewell My Concubine), (Famen Temple) (with Fu Ying), (Golden Platform) (with Xiaopei), and (Trial of Li Qi). All of them are masterpieces of his life. The metaphor of (Yellow Bell Dalu) can only be used by Shaoshan. There is nothing to be ashamed of.

Short News The candies and pastries of Sullivan in Shanghai are fragrant and linger in the mouth of the eater. Everyone praises them. Now there is a shop called Masikai next to the day and night bank in the Great World. Its food is so exquisite and wonderful that it is not only not below Sullivan, but it is no different from Sullivan. The eater thinks it is strange and asks the waiter. The waiter said that the big manager (that is, the cook) is from Sullivan. It is appropriate that they have different songs but the same work. Those who love sweets and pastries, why don't you try them? (Diner)

The Internal Politics of Post-War Poland (3) 164

— Sent from Paris by Li Liu-zeng

The local autonomy system stipulated by the new constitution should have been implemented everywhere on the same basis. However, the various legal systems adopted in different regions before the constitution was established could not be abolished immediately. Therefore, the first task of the legislators was to eliminate the most obvious differences in various regions and allow those who had not previously enjoyed autonomy to share the benefits. The provisional government specifically ordered the implementation of autonomy in Polish territories formerly under Russian rule, which is one example. This is because Polish territories formerly under German and Austrian rule had already enjoyed local autonomy due to the application of German and Austrian laws, while Polish territories formerly under Russian rule alone felt left out.

Therefore, the local autonomy in various parts of Poland is now implemented on different bases, and there is no unified system. The old German territory of Hante-Bilesie provides clear evidence, as its autonomous powers are particularly extensive due to a special decree.

Under these circumstances, the administrative unification of Poland is now maintained not by the laws themselves, but by the local officials who execute the central government's powers. Because local officials, such as county magistrates and town magistrates, can be arbitrarily transferred to their counties by the central government, from the old German Polish territories to the old Russian Polish territories, without restriction.

The establishment of Poland's administrative unity is inherently difficult, while its judicial unity is even more difficult. Poland has five different judicial systems nationwide. In the Warsaw (Warsaw) area, Napoleonic law is applied. In the eastern provinces, Russian law is applied. In other places, the laws of Germany, Austria, Hungary, and other countries are separately adopted. This is true for civil law, as well as for civil procedure law, commercial law, criminal law, and so on. Therefore, when Poland was restored, the regulations regarding family rights, mortgage systems, judicial evidence, and the identification of petty crimes were completely different from place to place.

Warmth in the Heart (273) 165

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Emerald Bamboo Tears Stain Her Face, Her Heart Breaks; Red Lotus Fragrance Fades, a Maiden's Soul Departs

For a man in his forties to take a concubine was considered an extremely proper thing in China. The main reason why Zhang Yiqing was able to move Cuiyun's heart and persuade her to marry him was one thing. He often told her, "Cuiyun, I won't lie to you. I do have a wife at home. But this wife is as good as nonexistent, because she is a country woman who is only fit to live in the countryside of Ningbo and not fit to come to Shanghai. That's why I've been doing business in Shanghai for more than twenty years, and she has never come once. They are used to living in the countryside and are not used to coming to Shanghai. However, once or twice a year, I go back to my hometown in Ningbo to see them. If you don't believe me, ask my friends. If you follow me, we'll rent a house in Shanghai. Every month, I'll take a boat to Hankou once or twice. We'll go together to see the scenery of the Yangtze River. Wouldn't that be great?" Although he said so, Cuiyun knew that the people of Ningbo called their wives "old women." And those Ningbo old women were very fierce. Last time, there was a young lady in her neighbor's room who took a customer, who was also from Ningbo. Somehow, her affair was leaked, and her old woman found out. That day, this customer happened to be staying in the next room on business. She found out about it. Early in the morning, she kicked down the door and caught them. The two of them were still entangled in bed. Unexpectedly, she broke into the room and dragged them both out of the covers. She didn't dare hit her own man, but she slapped the young lady and pulled out her hair. Her husband couldn't stand it and hit her too. She rolled on the ground, crying and shouting, "I don't want to live anymore! You're helping that whore to beat your old woman!" She shouted for the police to go to the police station together. That Ningbo woman was truly fierce. She rolled around on the floor for a while, her hair disheveled and her pants falling down. For a while, people from three or four rooms upstairs and downstairs came up to watch the commotion. Her husband saw that it was too embarrassing, put on his clothes, and ran away in a puff of smoke. Many people in the rooms tried to mediate, saying, "Your man isn't here. What are you still making a fuss about? We're hanging up signs to welcome guests. The Public Works Bureau collects donations for legitimate business. We didn't drag your man off the street. You can't control your own man, but you come here to make trouble. If you don't leave, we'll all go to the police station together. You won't get any advantage." She saw that her man had left too, so she smoothed her hair and tightened her belt, and walked downstairs cursing and shouting. She hired a rickshaw and left. The young lady in the next room felt she had lost face and made such a joke. She had suffered such hardship herself and was too embarrassed to see anyone. Unexpectedly, she ate raw opium. Fortunately, she was rescued early and saved her life.

Weaker Condition in Yarn Flower and Yarn Markets 171

The downward trend in the yarn market is due to the sharp decline in American cotton three-product yarn, which greatly disappointed bulls. Therefore, the local market is sluggish. However, the bulls of a certain manufacturer have always held on tightly, so the decline in wood yarn has not been drastic. However, the general trend of the world cotton industry is in this weakness and decline, and domestic wars are chaotic, with bandits rampant in all directions, sales have been greatly hit, so the bottom yarn inventory is accumulating daily. If transactions continue to stagnate like this, the subsequent decline will not stop.

Retreating Trend in Human Bidding. The human bidding opening price in the front market followed the trend of external cotton and declined, with the situation quite weak, each falling by one or two taels. In the second and third sessions, some profit-takers made up for a slight increase, each rising by two or three qian. As a result, each fell by seven, eight, nine qian to one tael and one qian. The afternoon market atmosphere was still weak, but the decline in three-product yarn was very strong, rising by nearly one qian and falling by two or three qian in the distant market. The total transaction volume for the day was 18,500 bales. Rongxing bought 1,600 bales, Yuda 1,100 bales, Yongfeng 1,400 bales, Yuantai 700 bales, and the remainder 300 to 500 bales. Hengyi sold 1,850 bales, Zhenda 1,250 bales, Yichang 1,050 bales, Gongtai 800 bales, Shenchang 650 bales, Gengfeng 600 bales, and others 300 to 550 bales. The closing prices of human bidding are recorded on the left.

Cotton Market is Extremely Soft and Declining 172

Sharp Decline in American Cotton··Great Disappointment for Bulls

The American cotton government report still reached 14,340,000 bales, a decrease of only 22,000 bales compared to the previous time, so cotton prices saw a sharp decline again, causing great disappointment for bulls in Shanghai. Retail buyers were quite alarmed. According to Japanese merchants, American cotton may continue to find new low prices. Spot cotton business has been cut off, and there is talk of cheap Indian cotton being mixed and sold, so there is no hope for the future of local cotton transactions. The harvest in Tongchong, Taicang, and other places is worse than in previous years, but Hubei is good, so a portion is being sold off vigorously. The cotton market is still difficult to stabilize under the decline of external cotton. However, the majority of people are holding on tightly due to the poor weather.

Han Bidding Falls by as Much as Four Qian. The opening price of Han bidding in the front market was quite weak. The majority of people's overnight purchases, seeing the sharp fall in American cotton, mostly turned from long to short. For a time, the situation was not good, each falling by four and a half qian. Later, manufacturers in Wuxi made up for it in large quantities, totaling more than 10,000 dan, slightly stabilizing the market. As a result, each fell by three and a half qian. The afternoon market atmosphere remained weak. Three-product cotton fell by one yuan and eight or nine jiao, and each month also fell by five fen. The total transaction volume for the day was 60,100 dan. Hengyi sold 6,900 dan, Taixing 3,400 dan, Shenchang 3,200 dan, Jinfeng 5,300 dan, Yuchang 3,400 dan, Tianchang 3,400 dan, and others 1,800 to 200. Hengde bought 10,900 dan, Yichang 3,000 dan, Yuanda 2,800 dan, Yongfeng 4,000 dan, and the remainder 1,200 to 2,500 dan. The closing prices of Han bidding are recorded on the left.

Grain River Downstream Rice Market Gradually Declines 175

Zhabei: Yesterday, the number of inland ships arriving at the source was moderate, and the traffic was relatively active. Although sales on this street were brisk, buyers unanimously demanded stricter quality, refusing to accept anything less than refined products. The arrival of Dongxin japonica rice was slightly more active, with prices slightly higher by half a yuan, opening at 17.5 yuan. Only goods from the downstream were available in the new Yangjian market, opening yesterday at 14.9 to 15.1 yuan. The arrival of new Kejian rice was very large, and sales were also smooth, with high-quality goods still opening at 14 yuan, and medium and lower grades down by 2 jiao. The market remained flat and sluggish. The Baiyuan market remained stable, due to the weak arrival of goods and smooth outbound traffic. Demand was very strong, and prices generally opened at 18.7 to 18.8 jiao.

South Shanghai: The arrival of river boats was still small. Sales on this street were average. High-quality broken japonica rice from the northern gang was still in short supply, so there was no standard price. A small amount of medium-grade japonica rice arrived, with prices rebounding slightly by a jiao or so. Dongxin japonica rice prices were slightly lower by 3 to 4 jiao, with market prices ranging from 17.5 to 17 yuan. Southern bang indica rice prices fluctuated. Although the sale of Bianyuan rice was active, the source of goods was dwindling. Jiangxi rice arrived successively, with prices slightly lower by 2 jiao.

Xiang Rice Handled by Qingdao Gang 176

A new batch of Huangqiao rice has arrived.

Yesterday, Ke Xian rice continued to arrive from Jiangxi, and a small batch was also shipped from Huangqiao Town in Jiangbei. Xiang rice has been officially unbanned, and large quantities are expected to arrive soon, so the market is quite sluggish. Fortunately, the demand on this street is still strong, and the Ke gang also has the Qingdao gang purchasing Huji Baoliang rice, so the market has turned from sluggish to better. The Tongshi sold more than 200 bags of Hunan Baoliang rice, priced at 11.83 to 11.75 yuan, and 350 bags of Ji Jing rice, priced at 13.05 to 12.95 yuan. 1,800 bags of Jiangxi early Ji rice, priced at 13.6, 13, and 12.5 yuan. 200 bags of late Ji rice, priced at 16.1 to 15.9 jiao. 186 bags of Huangqiao rice, priced at 12.2 jiao. Except for Xiang rice, which was handled by Qingdao, all were handled by this street.

Flat and Sluggish Market Situation 177

Yesterday, the wheat market remained flat and sluggish in both the morning and afternoon sessions. The quoted price of foreign wheat fell again by 3, 4, and 6 jiao. Some factories continued to gradually sell off their forward month contracts, so the overall sentiment was weak. However, the inland gang took advantage of this opportunity to buy in, so although the transaction volume was active, the decline was not as severe as the previous day. As a result, this month's price was slightly lower by 2 fen from the previous day, October's price was lower by 3 fen, November's price was lower by 2 fen, December's price was lower by 3 fen, and February's price was lower by 2 fen. The attitude of the factories in the current wheat market remains sluggish, because the sales of flour have not been active, so they remain conservative. It is feared that a further price reduction of 1 qian will be necessary.

Flour Market Still Weak 178

Yesterday's flour market was generally in a fluctuating state in both the morning and afternoon sessions. Although the quoted price of foreign wheat was slightly lower, the crux of the market seemed to be still in the hands of the factories. According to the current situation, the main food supply is loosening due to the bumper harvest, and flour is a supplementary food for the people, so it must follow the trend and fall. However, the buying and selling of standards has a fixed method, and the factories cannot release goods, which loses the possibility of adjustment. Therefore, in fact, the large factories must release their goods before the market can follow the environment. No factory releases were seen throughout the day, and the inland areas absorbed some, with only a slight difference in price. As a result, this month's price was lower by 2.5 li, October's price remained unchanged, November's price was lower by 2.5 li, December's price was lower by 7.5 li, January's price was lower by 5 li, and February's price was lower by 7.5 li.

Yesterday's sugar market production area telegrams: The current price of Cuban raw sugar is still 1.15625, New York futures sugar September is 1.10, December price is 1.18, next year March is 1.29, May is 1.38, comparing the previous telegrams there are no changes. The current price of Java raw sugar is 8.75, futures sugar September is 8.6875, October is 8.50, November is 8.375, compared to the previous also lacks rises and falls. The Guild market set the price of Dutch sugar 24 coarse granulated white aged goods at 8 liang, medium granulated white at 7 liang 6 qian, finely ground granulated white at 8 liang, transactions were also scarce, the market was flat and sluggish. Taikoo B Mark truck sugar was priced at 8 liang 1 qian 5 fen, Nissin Sugar YT Mark 8 liang 0 qian 7 fen 5 li, YRO Mark 7 liang 9 qian 5 fen, transactions were few, N Mark was quoted at 8 liang 1 qian 5 fen and lacked buyers. In fact, the daily arrivals turned abundant, and the sales in various places were sluggish, the buying atmosphere was bleak, and the market was very weak. The price of domestic Wufu ice sugar opened at 200 boxes, the price was still the original 6 liang 7 qian, the market was still firm. Since the huge amount of Dutch red sugar arrived, the market atmosphere suddenly turned depressed. Bingchang opened 2,000 bags of No. 8 goods, priced at 6 liang 3 qian, and at the same time, Huaxin quoted 6 liang 4 qian for No. 10 goods, and 6 liang 6 qian, and there were no inquiries.

Silk and Tea: Overseas Silk Sales Still Difficult to Progress 180

Yesterday, the silk market of foreign firms in this port still had difficulty progressing, because the price of Japanese silk in the European and American markets was very low, and although there were telegrams for Chinese silk, the price was still cheap. Chinese silk merchants' capital was not loose, and losses were too great, so all were watching and not moving forward. Yesterday, only 15 packs of top-grade Sichuan yellow factory silk from Mujiyang were opened, priced at 885 liang.

Large Tea Dealers in Luzhuang Slightly Active in American Sales 181

Yesterday, the Zhenmei tea from Luzhuang still showed a trend of rising and falling. Tianxiang and Yongxing and other firms continued to show strong interest in Wuyuan North Road tea and Tunxi core-drawn goods, and the selling prices did not rise or fall. Yesterday, the American firms in the Wuyuan Grand Company had already started handling the goods, but the selection was extremely strict, and the prices were very harsh. Most of the goods were sold in small quantities, and the remaining medium and low-grade goods, except for the Zhenmei item, which was slightly sold, the remaining 2 were all sluggish.

Shanghai Market

Business News 207

Since the opening of the Daxin Silk and Satin Bureau on East Xishi Road, Malu Road, it has been trusted by all circles for its genuine quality and low prices. Recently, the bureau is moving to a newly completed building and will hold a special grand sale of all its original goods from today onwards to thank all patrons for their years of patronage.

The Science Instrument Museum on Sijing Road, Qipan Street, announces that the museum will hold a grand sale at reduced prices for three weeks starting from September 8th. All physical and chemical instruments, chemical medicines, specimen models, surveying instruments, etc., will be sold at 10% off the original price. Fountain pens, writing brushes, drawing instruments, ink, colors, paper, lithographs, lithographic pencils, and other stationery, as well as musical instruments, are discounted to 40-50% of the original price, or sold at cost. This is an unprecedented price reduction, which is suitable for the opening of schools. Recently, the business at the door has been unusually crowded.

Theater News 208

The Paris Grand Theater announces that after autumn, this theater will exclusively show silent blockbusters that have never been shown in Shanghai. All details have been announced in the special notice advertisement of this theater. From today onwards, this theater will screen "The Flower Protector," starring big stars Betty Compson, Louis Stone, and Lee Quedis. The plot is bizarre and difficult to grasp, and the leading actors are veterans of the silver screen, so it is worth seeing.

The Lone Star Film Company announces that the chivalrous adventure agency blockbuster "Flying Swallow" recently produced by this company has been completed. The film is directed by Lu Fuyue, a filmmaker who studied in the United States. The plot is tortuous and compact, and the director's skill is superb. The leading actors are Qian Siying, Bao Gusong, and Zhang Lili, who perform delicately and admirably, fitting the plot. The scenery is rich and magnificent, and the literary scholar Cao Xuesong provides explanations. It is scheduled to be screened for three consecutive days at the Central Grand Theater on Six Ma Road, starting on the 18th of this month. At the same time, the Lone Star Theater Troupe will perform the new art-styled beauty drama "Xin Xiaoyaojin" on stage. They are rehearsing recently and are sparing no effort. It is predicted that there will be a grand occasion on the opening day.

Medical News 209

The American Food Company at No. 3 Guangdong Road announces that many patients suffer from stomach pain and indigestion, mostly due to excessive stomach acid and gas in the abdomen. Nowadays, people take soda to treat it, but it can only be effective for a while. Taking it for a long time will cause other problems. Recently, the American Biraishi Pharmaceutical Factory invented a kind of potion called Biraishi Stomach Water, which does not contain any soda. It is made by refining a kind of emulsion with other valuable items. Whether it is a new or old stomach disease, taking one bottle for minor cases and two bottles for major cases can cure it permanently. It is as effective as a god. Those with stomach problems should try it.

Publishing News 210

Chengzhen Society announces that the long-awaited first issue of Chengzhen has now been published. Although it is a thin booklet with only a few short articles, the authors' emotions, whether passionate or indifferent, can be fully revealed. The cover of this issue was made by a famous artist and is extremely beautiful. The members of this society are all students, so they bear the mission of promoting student literature and art. The first issue is now being distributed to all circles. If you want to request a copy by mail, please attach a three-cent stamp. Letters should be sent to the society's office at Nanyang Middle School, Longhua Road, Shanghai.

Automobile News

Commentary

American Newly Created Automobile Super Service Station 211

— Zhizheng

One-Stop System Benefits Car Owners, Comprehensive Preparations Reflect Motherly Care

Because the automobile industry is advancing rapidly and the various aspects related to automobiles are also developing rapidly, the most obvious is the automobile service station. This publication has already had a lot of discussion about automobile station services. Now the United States also has so-called "Super Service Station" organizations, and the content is becoming more scientific. Now, let's use two examples to illustrate this new product of automobiles.

The first successful Super Service Station was the Roland Automobile Company in Western Pennsylvania. Roland Company has two great buildings, one with five floors and one with three floors, occupying the center of the city and covering an area of ​​138,000 square feet. The company originally sold passenger cars. Buick, Mark, and Cadillac were all sold by him. Currently, he is shifting the focus from selling cars to Super Service Stations. He said in the advertisement that this Super Service Station is the largest and most complete in the world. In fact, it is well-deserved. Company Secretary Bairoko said that a Super Service Station can also be called "One-stop." What is a One-Stop? It means that no matter what kind of car comes, whether it is a minor problem or a major repair, whether it needs parts or manufacturing, everything can be handled here. There is no need to go to a second place to deal with it. Isn't it true that after "one-stop," you don't need to stop again?

The five-story building is now dedicated to selling cars, while the three-story building is dedicated to Super Service Stations. Although the work is clearly divided between the two buildings, every car that enters the car sales area must pass through the Super Service Station. The gate is on the left. Inside is the accounting and battery room. On the right is the office of the company's general manager. The Super Service Station is inside. The first item is a car wash machine, using extremely new-style machinery. The second item is a brake and lubrication testing machine. At the same time, tire and battery repair machines are also installed. The light in the room is exceptionally clear, and there is no need for lights for repairs. On the second floor, there is a car painting area. The repair shop covers an area of ​​about 9,600 square feet. On the door of the lubrication area, there is a slogan written in large characters: "Lubricate Your Car."

The Super Service Station only opened on May 3rd. That was the company's 25th anniversary. In the past 25 years, the company has actually become the largest company in Western Pennsylvania. Speaking of the company's history, it is also interesting. When it was opened in 1907, its position was not even half of what it is now. It was not until June 1912 that it bought some land. It was not until 1916 that two buildings were built. Two years later, the company's affairs developed, and the buildings were renovated. Since the success of the Super Service Station, business has become more and more wonderful. Everyone entrusts all their affairs to him because he has perfect equipment. He—the Super Service Station—is truly the mother of automobiles.

The second case is in California. The company's name is "Calideu." His Super Service Station is built very uniquely. The machines include car washing, lubrication, car testing, and light testing, etc. In addition, there are also restaurants, barbershops, art shops, etc. for car owners to enjoy. The owner of "Calideu" company said, "Now what car owners value most is not repair, but maintenance. The so-called maintenance includes car lubrication, car testing, and car types. Facts tell us that the repair cost for a car owner in the first year of buying a car is only one-third or one-quarter of the maintenance cost. After three years, the repair cost gradually increases. However, at that time, it has become an old car. Setting up a service station by the car seller is especially convenient for the car owner. The car seller understands the car owner's situation and still provides free maintenance for a certain period. What our company emphasizes is this point. Since the establishment of the Super Service Station, the results have been extremely satisfactory. We are working hard to move forward."

In short, the differences between a Super Service Station and an ordinary service station are roughly two points. First, a Super Service Station has a larger scope and more complete equipment. Second, a Super Service Station can handle all the affairs of customers. No matter how damaged it is, it can handle it all.

Studebaker New Style 212

Automatic shifting. Free Wheeling is the latest invention for the Studebaker President and Commander eight-cylinder new cars. Not only does it enhance their already established smoothness and stability, but the car owner can use this device to shift gears at will at 40 to 50 miles per hour without ever using the clutch. No sound, extremely convenient. With this device, the car's mileage record is not enough to affect the engine because, as a result, the wear and tear on the engine, rear axle, and power transmission are all avoided, and the consumption of gasoline and oil is greatly reduced. It is said that the Hengmao Automobile Company has already shipped these new cars and displayed them at No. 23 McTyeire Road, where the company's new sample room welcomes people from all walks of life to visit and appreciate them. (Yun)

Page 27

Well organized, so it is also called the "One-Stop" system. Since the automotive industry has had the Super Service Station organization, everyone entrusts their cars to them to save time. They maintain the cars with the heart of a loving mother caring for her children. They complement each other, and the demand for setting up super service stations has gradually spread throughout the United States. (September 7th, at Jiaotong University)

The Jiangzhe Managerial United Association of Texaco Oil Company of America held a farewell banquet for Mr. Shi Daban of the Shanghai Department returning to his country and welcomed the acting Mr. Meng Daban on August 30th at the Great China Hotel, followed by a group photo.

Automobiles and the Northwest (Part 1) 213

— Xiao Yuan

The Northwest region, from Suiyuan extending northwest, connecting Mongolia, southwest and the three provinces of Xin, Gan, and Shaanxi, occupies tens of thousands of miles. It is a desolate area, sparsely populated, but rich in resources and treasures, a truly God-given region. This often arouses the covetousness of foreigners, who constantly think of seizing it. Since Red Russia's invasion of Mongolia, the situation on the frontier has become increasingly urgent. The sudden pressure has stirred the nation's sense of fear. Recently, private individuals or groups have even organized Northwest travel groups, but due to inconvenient transportation and bandits everywhere, government offices often exaggerate the danger and do not take responsibility for safety. This has led those with lofty aspirations for travel to go no further than Baotou, near the tomb of Wang Zhaojun (in Suiyuan city, there is the tomb of Wang Zhaojun, called Mingfei Mound). As for the fertile fields of Wuyuan, the area of the Hetao pastures, and the living conditions of the Mongolian banners and border people, all are inaccessible due to traffic congestion, making it impossible to set foot among them, to see with one's own eyes, and to achieve the merit of on-the-spot investigation. However, private groups are actually concerned about the desert. Their ambition and courage are enough to make people admire and be amazed. Moreover, since then, the advocacy for managing the Northwest has suddenly and unexpectedly become loud again in the dust of the old capital. Although actual visits may not be scheduled, this promotion is enough to show that our people have never forgotten the Northwest for a single day. It also prompts the government to pay attention to it. What is regrettable is that private groups are ultimately too weak, only able to run around and call for support for a while. Their backing still needs a strong and powerful government. However, today's government, due to the many difficulties of the current situation and the shortage of financial resources, still finds it difficult to stop internal construction. How can it have the spare energy to take care of other things? In the end, this rich and fertile land will never be developed and will be abandoned, giving foreigners a chance to covet it, while patriotic people in the country have no strategy to ask about it. Speaking of this, one cannot help but sigh. It is recently heard that Chairman Li Hanchu is quite able to invigorate those with the ambition to manage it. Recently, he established a bureau in Atao Banner (west of Wuyuan) to govern the area, and the director, Gao Ziqian, is an old acquaintance of mine and is quite capable. In the future, he will manage and build in the desolate deserts and lush forests, establishing a glorious and extraordinary achievement and adding an unparalleled glory to the Republic of China. Then, the future of the Northwest can be hoped for.

The only policy for managing the Northwest is to resettle people there as soon as governance is established. With the people moving in, the border will be secured. On one hand, encourage cultivation and development of mineral resources. On the other hand, promote animal husbandry and expand the sale of fur. If these are successful, then after a year, the products and output of the Northwest will definitely increase, and the income of the Northwest will be more than enough to support the people of the Northwest. When the country looks west, there will be no financial difficulties to worry about. However, the policy of resettlement places the greatest emphasis on transportation. Without adequate transportation, banditry cannot be eliminated. If the bandits are not suppressed, the people will not dare to come. Even if they come, they cannot settle down. If they are not at peace, they cannot stay long. Coming today and leaving tomorrow, how is that different from not resettling at all? There are various designs for transportation, but the most important thing to implement first is the safety and convenience of travelers and the railway industry. However, in the vast wilderness, the planning of the route cannot be done in a short time, and the financial resources are especially beyond the reach of today's government. Even if the Ping-Sui Railway is used to extend to Dingkou or Ningxia, although it is no more than a thousand miles long, the cost of rails and locomotives is not light. Thinking and planning in silence, this is not an easy task. Moreover, with the national treasury so empty, how can it be easy to talk about? The next best thing is the automobile. The capital for automobiles is lighter, and road construction is easier. The other conditions are also quite simple. Therefore, according to my ideal, transportation in the Northwest must first start with automobiles, so that things will be easier to do and easier to see success. If a railway must be planned, it is a fundamental plan, but in the end, it will be necessary to borrow foreign debt.

In the past, when Feng Huanzhang was the Director-General of Northwest Border Defense, he stationed troops in Baotou (the westernmost point of the Ping-Sui Railway, which is also very interested in planning for Northwest transportation. His original plan was to build a trunk line along the Houtao to Dingkou, and then cross the Hetao to Ningxia to form a second trunk line. From these two trunk lines, several branch lines would then be extended to places such as Wuceng, Linhe, and Kushui Lake. After the branch lines were successful, several short lines would then be formed to the important tribes in Inner Mongolia, still converging on the two trunk lines. The plan was not without grandeur, and troops had already been moved to start construction. Although the operation was arduous, the project was completed for the most part in a few months. The determination cannot be said to be without the greatest perseverance. Who knew that financial resources would be strained and the country would have many affairs? Before it could be completed, Feng had left the country. When the Battle of Nankou was lost and the entire army retreated west, all the automobiles were used to transport long-distance military supplies. After driving west, they never returned. The automobile road, which had been painstakingly built for several months with the blood and sweat of countless soldiers, was also completely trampled by the wheels and hooves of the retreating army. In recent years, although the Suiyuan authorities have also made plans, during the military period, local finances are even more difficult, and there is still much that cannot be done in administrative construction. It is even more impossible to talk about transportation in the wilderness. Since the officials are powerless, the merchants do not come forward. The people are dissatisfied, and bandits swarm together. Murder and robbery are heard every day. Travelers are especially wary, and the desolation of the Northwest may be even worse than in those years. This has made the excellent agricultural and animal husbandry fields and the rich land of heaven and earth allow foreigners to covet and seize it, and compete to implement their aggressive ambitions. The Book says, "A common man is not guilty, but he is guilty for possessing treasure." The fierce neighbors are watching intently, which is enough to make the troubled people of the country feel anxious. If there is still no overall and concrete plan within a few years, I am afraid that the border troubles in the Northwest will be a painful thing to say.

The transportation that the Northwest already has relies only on the Ping-Sui Railway, which goes west to Baotou. From Baotou to the west and south, the navigation of the Houtao can still be used. As for the trend, the Northwest has no other means except for the labor of cattle and horses. When sailing upstream against the wind, it takes more than twenty days to reach Dingkou from Baotou. As for the labor of cattle and horses, it is even more unreliable. When the weather is good and there is no wind or rain, a horse cannot travel more than a hundred miles a day. Cattle can only travel about sixty miles. Although automobiles can travel five hundred miles a day, long-distance wind and snow and light rain are not harmful. Comparing the two, the distance an automobile travels in a day can be compared to the distance a horse or cattle travels in one to five or ten, and it can be compared to a boat in one to fifteen. There is already such a benefit in terms of time, and there are also equal benefits in terms of economy. Once transportation is convenient, everything in the area becomes convenient. The residents and merchants of the interior will come without being invited. How can the Northwest's businesses be limited? Although this is close to ideal, it can be put into practice, how can it not be so? From this, we know that automobiles are not only of considerable value in the future development of the Northwest, but also have the ability to connect the merchants and travelers who travel to and from Shaanxi and Suiyuan in the present.

Automobiles occupy a considerable position in Northwest transportation. However, those who engage in this business are merchants who take profit as their aim, and their capital is at stake. Who would be willing to waste it? At a time when banditry has not been quelled and there are thorns and weeds along the way, if the government does not have considerable measures to provide them with effective protection, I am afraid that merchants will not be able to invest without worry. Therefore, transportation in the Northwest must first start with bandit suppression. If the bandits are eliminated, transportation will be unimpeded, merchants and people can be without fear, and the Northwest can be greatly developed. Those who operate automobiles will also be eager to invest. In my opinion, now is the time for the government to do its best to suppress bandits, while dividing troops to repair roads, planning resettlement, and raising several hundred thousand yuan to organize a convenient transportation agency. Allow merchants to invest and cooperate, and the government is in a supervisory position. Merchants should get their share of the profits, and the government should take it to maintain the roads. If we plan like this, it may be sustainable. Merchants will also have no way to hoard and speculate to exploit travelers. Travelers will praise the convenience, and officials and merchants will have no worries about capital. Transportation may be expected to develop.

Road Administration in the Three Cities of Anqing, Wuhu, and Bengbu in Anhui Province 215

— Wu Fei

Although the three cities of Anqing, Wuhu, and Bengbu in Anhui Province are experiencing economic difficulties, the progress of road administration is still rapid. Recently, the new construction of roads in Anqing City, the repair and expansion of roads in Wuhu City, and the widening of streets in Bengbu City are very important for the appearance of the city. The following is a detailed description:

Anqing City Adds Two Roads to the Sida Station. Now that the Anqing-Qiantai Road is open to traffic, the route is developing day by day, and there are more and more pedestrians. The prosperity of the new city has begun. In addition, the development of the new city area in the eastern suburbs is entrusted to the new life of Anqing City. The development of the new city area must be linked to the old city. The planned two roads of the Sida Station are the backing for the implementation of this plan. The Sida Road is 85 feet long and 38 feet wide. The six projects including roadbed, curb stone, water pipe, road surface, moat culvert, and sidewalk require 3,000 yuan and 6 yuan. The station road is 50 feet long and 38 feet wide. The six projects including roadbed, curb stone, water pipe, road surface, moat culvert, and sidewalk require 2,604 yuan and 25 cents. The cost is slightly higher than Sida.

Wuhu City Repairs the North Road and Widens the Streets. In Wuhu City, the section from Tiefosi to the Customs Wharf is extremely narrow. The City Engineering Bureau is now designing and building it. From the power company to the Customs Wharf, including North Road and the original Zhongjiang Road, it is 1,500 meters long. The project is divided into two sections. The first section starts in front of Tiefosi and ends in front of Xingwuli, with a total of 2,342 English squares of earth filling. The second section starts at the Shandong Road intersection and ends in front of the Hengshengli of the original Zhongjiang Road, with a total of 4,892 English squares of earth filling. The earth filling project is transported by light rail. All light rail tracks, sleepers, iron nails, and earth-carrying iron cars are supplied by the bureau, but the track laying work is borne by the contractor. In addition, the roads in the Erjie area are the main transportation routes in Wuhu City, but the roads are narrow and the ditches are silted up, so they should be widened and dredged separately to revitalize road administration. It is stipulated that the width of the two streets is 50 English feet, and the middle lane is 30 English feet. The sidewalks on both sides are each 16 English feet wide. The most important thing in municipal facilities is roads. Not only is it related to the neatness of the city, but it is also related to the progress of commerce. Therefore, the narrow Erjie will be widened and dredged.

Bengbu City Revises the Method of Widening Streets. Bengbu City's ban on the construction of houses by citizens has always been handled in accordance with the building rules approved by the Public Security Bureau. Now that the original rules are not perfect, according to the provisions of the City Organization Law, referring to the Nanjing City's method of widening streets, and taking into account the situation of Bengbu City, the Engineering Bureau has formulated eight articles of temporary regulations on widening streets and retreating houses. It has been approved and promulgated by the Municipal Preparatory Office and stipulates six types of road widths, with the widest being 30 meters and the narrowest being 7 meters. Complementing the original old rules, it not only improves the streets but also regulates road administration, and is a key plan for developing the new city.
